And when the sore is in a place which can be removed, as we have said, it is that you purge the patient with black bile; then make him satiated if there is manifest repletion, then open the sore gently 1 inch wide to perform the operation; then cut the flesh of the sore, and the skin and fat from all around it, leaving nothing behind; and let the blood flow out freely, and press the wound with your hand or something else, and if the bleeding from the artery or vein causes a pulse, cauterize it until the pulse stops; then treat the wound further until it is healed.
de ydropisie	of dropsy
Nos avons jai dit en la division les semblances d’idropisie, et en queil maniere li assemblee de l’aigue est faite, et les signes de chescune semblance, et la cure qui est faite par medicines, et cele qui est curee par fer: si est eclites soulement; et ne doit on touchier de fer en ces .ij. semblances: c’est a savoir, tympanites et yposarche, car c’est mortelz chose; donques quant tu medicines ceste semblance de ydropisie qui est apelee «eclites» de medicines, et li cure ne profite, si regarde se li malaides est foibles, ou s’il ait autre maladie que ydropisie, si com toust et solution de ventre et semblans choses; si n’i touchier de fer, car il i a doutance; et se tu vois le malaide de fort vertut, et il n’a autre maladie que ydropisie soulement, et il n’est mie trop jones ne trop vielz, si dois ensi ovrer:	We have already discussed in the division of similarities the appearance of dropsy, and how the accumulation of fluid occurs, and the signs of each similarity, and the treatment through medicine, and that which is cured by iron; so let it be known only; and you must not use iron for these two appearances: that is to say, tympany and hydrops, because they are deadly; therefore when you treat this appearance of dropsy called "eclites" with medicine, and the cure does not help, then consider if the patient is weak, or if they have another illness besides dropsy, such as stomach pain and similar things; in these cases, do not use iron, for there is doubt; and if you see that the patient is very strong and only has dropsy, and is neither too young nor too old, then you should act thus:
lieve le malaide droit sus tes mains, et li ministres presse le ventre em boutant l’aigue a la plus basse partie dou pis, puis pren le spatumile espinous selonc ceste forme: Et soit trenchans de .ij. pars. a pointe, et toutevoie ne soit mie si entrans qu’il puist venir jusc’a l’intestine quant on le fiche ens, et ne le puist blecier;	gently lay the patient flat on his back, and press his stomach upwards to push the fluid to the lowest part of the abdomen near the groin, then take a spiny spathum according to this form: And let it be as thin as 2 parts at the tip, and yet not so sharp that it would pierce through to the intestines when it is inserted, nor so blunt that it won't go in;
puis regarde se li ydropisie est enjanree devers les intestines: si covient que tu fendes ensus de la boude .iij. dois droit desoz sus lou poignil; et se li ydropisie est por la maladie dou foie, si soit ta fendure au senestre de la boude .iij. dois; et se c’est por la miuce, si soit a destre, et ne covient mie que li malaides gise sus la fendure que les superfluitez ne corrent a celui foible leu;	then check if the dropsy is located near the intestines: in that case, you must split open below on the palm side of the index finger 3 times directly; and if the dropsy is due to liver disease, then the split should be on the left side of the palm; and if it is due to kidney disease, then on the right, and the patient must not lie on the split so that the excess fluid does not flow into that weak area.
puis perce tout le cuir a l’estrument, et le boute, et lieve ta main a tout le spatumile entre le cuir et le syfac ausi com en escorchant a la quantiteit d’une ungle ou enqui entor; puis perce lou syfac tant que li spatumile viegne au leu vuit, et c’est li leus de l’aigue, puis le trai fuer, et i boute cest estrument de coi ci est li forme: Et est semblans a une caine d’argent subtil, et est d’arain ou d’archaut legier, et a en la partie desoz .i. petit pertus; et ou costeit d’une part, .iij. pertus; et .ij. d’autre part, et .i. d’autre; et est li chiés tailliez si com une penne, et c’est li forme de l’incision dont li escrivains taille la penne:	then pierce the entire skin with the instrument, and fill it up, and release your hand over the entire spatumile between the skin and the syphac as though scraping off in the quantity of a fingernail or so; then pierce the syphac until the spatumile reaches the desired location, and that is the place for the water; then draw it out, and insert this instrument from which comes the shape: And it is similar to a silver needle, and is made of lightweight copper or bronze, and has in the lower part a small hole; and on one side, three holes; and two on the other, and one on another; and the head is cut like a feather, and that is the shape of the incision from which scribes cut the pen:
au chief desus est li alemele, si que quant li estrumens vient a l’aigue, si dessent maintenant sus l’estrument; vuide la donques la moitiet ou la tierce part, car se tu en vuides plus qu’il ne covient en celle houre, par aventure si muert li malaides por la resolution de son esperit de l’arme, ou il chiet paumez, ou il aproche a la mort;	at the top of which is the alemele, so that when the instrument reaches the water, it falls immediately upon the instrument; empty it therefore by half or by a third, for if you empty more than is proper in that hour, by chance the patient may die from the shock to his spirit, or he will faint, or he will come close to death;
mais en vuide selonc la quantiteit de sa vertut, et selonc ceu que les dispositions de la vertut dou malaide signifient, et ses poulz; puis trai l’estrument et retien l’aigue, et elle est retenue maintenant por le keur qui estoupe le pertus qui est sus le syfac, de coi j’ai parleit, que tu perces selonc ceste maniere; puis rencomence l’estrument l’autre jor, se tu vois le malaide soffrant ceu, et trai de l’aigue une petite quantiteit;	but empty it according to the amount of his strength, and according to what the disposition of his strength indicates, and his pulses; then draw out the instrument and retain the water, which is now retained by the membrane that blocks the hole which is above the syphac, about which I have spoken, that you pierce in this manner; then begin again with the instrument the next day if you see the patient suffering from this, and draw off a small amount of water;
fai ce aucun jor, et te garde de foloier tant qu’il ni demore mais c’un poc d’aigue. Et se tu doutes sus le malaide, et tu i lais mout d’aigue, si le cure de la sepulture ou sablon chaut, et par mout sueir ou bain et au soleil, et se teigne de boivre; et le cure de medicines desiccatives tant qu’il soit sanez, et cauterize sus l’estomac et sus lou foie et sus l’esplen aprés l’estraction de l’aigue, si com j’ai dit devant.	do this for a few days and avoid bathing until it is completely healed. And if you doubt the wound, leave it with a lot of water, then treat it with hot earth or sand, and through sweating in a bath and in the sun, and by drinking; and treat it with medications to dry it up until it heals, and cauterize over the stomach and liver and spleen after the extraction of the pus as I have said before.
de l’estopement de la verge	of the swelling of the penis
Aucune fois naissent enfant qui n’ont point de pertus en la verge, ou li pertus est petis, ou il n’est mie en son leu. Si le covient tantost qu’il n’aist percier a tout .i. spatumile molt subtil selonc ceste forme: puis met ou pertus .i. clo subtil de plonc, et le lie et le tien ensi .iij. jors ou iiij. et quant il vuet faire urine, si soit ostez li clos, et faice urine, et puis li remet; et par aventure nen i couvient point, car li urine qui vient fuer ne lou laisse close.	Sometimes children are born without an opening on the penis, or the opening is small and not in the right place. Then one must immediately pierce it with a very thin spatulum according to this form: then put into the opening a very thin plug of lead, and ligate it and leave it for three or four days, and when he wants to urinate, remove the plug and let him urinate, and then replace it; and perhaps it is not necessary at all, because the urine that comes out does not allow it to close.
Cil de cui li pertus est petis, si est medicinez dou clo de plonc, si com nos avons dit, si s’eslargera. Cil qui n’ont mie le pertus en lor leu sont bleciet, car aucun naissent qui ont le pertus au chief de la verge, por coi il ne puient pissier avant s’il ne lievent lor verge en haut; et ne pueent enjanrer por ceu que li matiere ne puet venir jusc’a la marris, et c’est une male maladie.	Those with a small opening will be helped by the plug of lead, as we have said, and it will enlarge. Those who do not have the opening in its place are blighted, for some are born with the opening at the tip of the penis, and because of this they cannot urinate before they lift their penis upward; and they cannot ejaculate because the material cannot reach the testicles, and this is a serious illness.
Et li maniere de l’ovraige si est que li malaides gise sovin sus son dos, puies estent le chief de la verge et le cope ausi com la taille d’une penne, si ke li pertus chiece em mileu, si com il covient; et te garde de decorrement de sanc qui i vient maintes fois, et s’il avient, si l’estainche de ceu qui estainche sanc, et cure la plaie tant qu’il soit sanez.	And the way to do it is for the patient to lie on his back, then the head of the penis and the foreskin are cut to the size of a feather, so that the opening is in the middle, as it should be; and beware of bleeding which often occurs, and if it does, stanch the flow of blood, and treat the wound until it heals.
des pustules de la verge	of the penis
Maintes fois vienent cist albathe en la verge, et est une apparance de char laide; et en i a malignes et non malignes; si covient que tu les preignes a .i. oncine subtil, et les cope et munde toutes, puis met sus coton moilliet en oignement egiptien; puis le cure d’oignement diafinicon tant qu’il soit sanez.	Many times these blisters come on the penis, and they have an unattractive appearance; and there are both malignant and non-malignant ones; so you must grasp them with a small, sharp knife, and cut away and clean all of them, then put on wet cotton soaked in Egyptian ointment; then treat it with diafinicon ointment until it is healed.
Et se li albathe est maligne, de pute color et depuant, si covient que tu i amenistres cautere. Quant tu l’as copeit, et se li albathe est en som la verge, et en ait partie dedens la peil et partie defuer, si covient que tu oste l’albathe qui est dedens premier; et quant il est soudez, si le cure defuer. Car quant tu le cures ensamble, si n’est mie asseurez li chiez de la verge qu’il ne soit perciez, et vient noiror et corruption en son la verge et ou coion; si covient chever tout ceu qui est noir et corrumput, puis lie sus l’emplaustre de miel et de farine qui soit fait d’escorce de poumes grenates et de veces, puis le cure d’autres cures tant qu’il soit sanez.	And if the blister is malignant, discolored and suppurating, then cauterize it. When you have cut it, and if the blister is on the shaft of the penis, with part of it inside the skin and part outside, then you must first remove the blister that is inside; and when it is sutured, treat the outside. For if you treat them both together, there is not assured that the skin of the penis will not be pierced, and blackness and corruption can come into his penis and testicles; so cut away all that is black and腐, then apply an ointment made of honey and flour from pomegranate peel and rosebuds, then treat it with other treatments until it is healed.
Et se decorremens de sanc vient, si amenistre le cautere lunaire selonc ceste forme: Li cauteres si aide as .ij. dispositions ensamble: c’est asavoir, au decorrement de sanc, et a la corruption; et se li chiés de la verge est corrumpus et retrais, si covient que tu boutes ou conduit de la verge une cainne de plonc, et pisse li malaides parmi; et quant li pelz iert aerse au chief de la verge qui avient a ces qui n’ont mie esteit circoncis, ou il avient por plaie ou por aposteme, si covient donques que tu l’escorches a .i. estrument cheveit, tant que li liiens soit desliiez, et soit delivrez li chiez de la verge de toutes pars;	And if there is bleeding, then apply the lunar cautery according to this form: The cautery has two functions together: that is, for bleeding and for corruption; and if the head of the penis is corrupted and withdrawn, then you should insert a tube into the urethra and let the patient urinate; and when there is a discharge at the tip of the penis which happens to those who have not been circumcised, or due to a wound or abscess, then you must scrape it with a sharp instrument until the foreskin is detached and the head of the penis is completely exposed.
et se c’est grief chose de deviser ceu, si covient que tu l’escorches a .i. spatumile aucun poc dou chief de la verge et de la peil; puis dessevre belement entre .ij., et i met .i. subtil drapeil de lin moilliet an aigue froide, qu’il n’aerse derechief. de la circoncision	On circumcision:
Circoncision n’est mie desliemens de continuation si com les autres plaies; toutevoie quant nos faison ceste oevre de nostre volenteit, et proprement as enfans, si est mestier que nos faisiens la millor oevre, et la plus legiere a salut.	Circumcision is not like other wounds in that it does not heal on its own; nevertheless, when we perform this procedure intentionally, especially on children, we must do the best and least harmful job.
Je dis que li ancien ne dirent mie la circoncision de lor enfans, car il n’en usent mie en lor loi, et n’en avons mais que ceu que nos avons aquis par experiment.	I say that the ancients did not speak of the circumcision of their children, for they did not use it in their law, and we have no more than what we have acquired by experience.
Car j’ai veut la plus grant partie des maistres et des sainors qui faisoient circumcision entor .i. dal, et as forces, et a tout une novacule; si fuioit li keurs car il i a .ij. toiles, et par aventure si cope on celi desus et demore celle desoz.	For I have seen the greater part of masters and surgeons who made circumcision around the foreskin, and in many places, and on any new-born; then the hymen would be cut because there are two membranes, and sometimes one is cut above and the other remains below.
Or la recovient coper, et est li dolor double, et a la mundification qui est dou dal n’est mie asseuree li pointe dou membre; et a la mundification de l’ungle par aventure eschaipe li fer, et corront l’uevre, et maintes fois naissent ensi qu’il n’ont mestier de mundification et je l’ai veut.	Now they recover quickly, and the pain is doubled, and in the cleaning which is done to the foreskin is not secure the tip of the member; and in the cleaning of the nail sometimes the iron slips and they ruin the work, and many times are born thus that they do not need cleaning, and I have seen it.
De la mondification qui est faite as forces a tout le liien de fil ai je troveit la bonteit de l’experiment, car les forces taillent justement ausi bien desus com desoz.	Of the cleaning that is done to the foreskin all over the thread I have found the goodness of the experiment, for the forces cut justly above as below.Or li fuit li doler qui tailla l’ungle, si doit il le tailler par fin et non pas par costé, car par fin il ne se peult mander; si doit il estre tailli par costé, et il faut qu’il soit tailli tant qu’il eschieve la chair.
Car quant tu presses ta main, si tailles igalment en .i. tout soul tens; mais que li filz soit bien estrois entor lou cuir; et soit li maniere dou premier ovraige si est que tu faices penser l’enfant, s’il entent, que tu ne li fais fuer que liier le fil entor la verge tant soulement, et pues le fai esjoir en toutes les manieres que tu pues;	For when you press your hand, you cut evenly into the skin all around; but the thread must be wrapped tightly around the penis; and the method of the first operation is such that if the child understands, you make him believe that you are only tying the thread around the penis, and then you make him urinate in every way you can.

Li forme des forces a la mundification si est ceste: li dui chiés soient tenves et soient trenchans, et soient li chiés ausi grant com li mainche igalment:	The form of the foreskin after cleansing should be as follows: the two foreskins should be thin and pointed, and the foreskin should be as large as the palm of the hand evenly.

dou retenement de l’urine	from the retention of urine:
Li retenue de l’urine si est d’opilation de piere, ou de sanc congeleit, ou de bowe, ou de char nee, ou de semblans choses, que nos avons dit en la division;	The retention of urine is due to the obstruction of a stone, or frozen blood, or a tumor, or a foreign body, or similar objects which we have mentioned in the classification.
et se li urine n’est desliie, et tu vois estre la retenue por la piere qui est jai ou col de la vessie, si covient que li malaides soit corbés sus ses genoulz; et li soient mis li piez sor le dos, et estende son ventre de la partie desus lou dos, et restraigne li malaides s’alainne tant com il puet; et adonques est constrains li colz de la vessie a l’expression de la piere au desus, por coi li urine est desliie e;	If the urine is not released, and you see that it is retained due to a stone lodged in the neck of the bladder, then the patient should be made to bend his knees, and have his feet placed on his back, and press his abdomen from above the back, and restrain himself as much as he can; this will force the neck of the bladder to express the stone upwards, causing the urine to be released.

de la piere	of stone

de la piere des femmes	of women's stone
Poc avient que piere soit enjanree en femmes, et s’il avient aucune fois, si est li cure grief, et est deffendut por .iij. choses: l’une est que per aventure li femme est vierge; et li seconde est c’on ne puet trover femme bien saichant qui se descuevre as mires, meismement quant elle est caste.	It sometimes happens that stone is lodged in women's bodies, and if it does, the cure is difficult due to three reasons: one is that the woman might be a virgin; the second is that one cannot find a woman who is knowledgeable enough to examine them, especially when she is chaste.
Et li tierce maniere si est que par aventure on ne puet trover femme bien saichant en cest art de mains; et li quarte maniere si est que li piere de la femme si est plus em parfont que li piere de l’ome, por coi il i couvient faire plus parfonde taille, et grant paour i a.	The third reason is that one might not be able to find a skilled female practitioner in this art of medicine; and the fourth is that women's stones are often deeper than men's, requiring deeper incisions, which causes great fear.
Et se necessitez semont a ceu, si covient que tu preignes une mieresse bien sachant, et a poines la trueve on, et se tu n’en trueves, point si quier .i. caste mire subtil; et li presente une baile bien saige en la vie des femmes, ou une femme qui saiche une partie de l’art, et li comande qu’ele faice ceu que tu li comandes de l’inquisicion de la piere;	And if one needs to do so, they should take a skilled midwife, and with her, a wise old woman who knows about women's bodies, or a woman who understands part of the art, and command them to do what you command regarding the examination of the stone.
et regarde mout bien se li femme est vierge: adonques li covient bouter son doit ou fondement et querir la piere; et s’ele la trueve, si la constraigne desoz son doit, et li recomande qu’elle boute son doit ou con la malaide, et quiere et presse sa main senestre sus la vessie forment.	and look very carefully to see if the woman is a virgin; then she should push her finger into her vagina and search for the stone; and if she finds it, she should hold it under her finger, and recommend that she pushes her finger into her vagina with the disease, and searches and presses her left hand firmly on her bladder.

puis cure la plaie d’autre cure, tant qu’il soit sanez parfaitement.	Then treat the wound with another treatment until it is perfectly healed.Et quant il sont sanez, si met sur li liien ou cautere de feu, et les remue ains qu’il se muevent, et remettant li lius en son leu.
de hernie carnouse	of carnous hernia
En ceste ramice ne vis je onques nul qui osast faire la cure par fer.	In this chapter I have never seen anyone dare to perform the treatment with iron.
Et li ancien dirent qu’ele est faite si com li ramice qui est ensamble la vis, en teil maniere que tu lie les vasselz, aprés la taille sus ous legierement au desoz;	And the ancients say that it is made like the ramus which is together with the vein, in such a way that you tie the vessels, after cutting above and lightly underneath;
puis cope em mi, et cure l’aposteme de ceu qui oevre, tant que li vasselz chient; et le cure si com nos avons dit, tant qu’il soit sanez.	then cut into it halfway, and cure the abscess of him who opens it, until the vessels leak; and cure it as we have said, until he is healed.
Aucune fois vient routure ens angres, si com nos avons dit, et apert li leus; et ne dessent nulz des intestines as coions, et s’il en i dessent, c’est poc, et repaire toutes houres;	Sometimes the wound opens into the bowels, as we have said, and the place is exposed; and none of the intestines should come out with the faeces, and if they do, it is a little bit, and it heals within hours;
et toutevoie s’il demoure trop en cest point, si croit li plaie ou syphac, tant que li intestine dessent;	and yet if he remains too long in this state, the wound or ulcer will suppurate until the intestines protrude;
et ceu avient par l’estension dou syfac qui est as angres, si com nos avons dit, car il est estendus, puis est mollifiez et enflez li leus et apert;	and this happens because of the extension of the ulcer which is at the angles, as we have said, for it extends and then becomes soft and swollen and open;
et li cure si est par cautere, si com nos avons devant dit; et aucune fois est curee par fer en ceste maniere:	and the treatment is with a cautery, as we have already said. Sometimes it is treated with iron in this way:
et est que li malaides gise sovin sus son dos entre tes mains, puis cope le leu de la routure enfleit dou large selonc la quantiteit de .iij. dois;	and let the patient lie on his back between your hands, then fill the wound with salt according to its size, about a quarter of a pound;
et puis estrai le syfac qui est desoz le cuir que l’ensuet, puis pren lou rait et lou met sor le leu apparant dou syfac;	and then extract the boil which is under the skin, then take the thread and place it over the visible spot of the boil;
et lou presse au parfont dou ventre, puis cout les .ij. leus apparans dou syfac sus lou chief dou rait, et cout l’un et l’autre;	and press it deeply into the belly, then tie the two ends of thread visible over the boil on the head of the thread, and tie them one and then the other;
puis estrai le chief dou rait, et ne coper point dou syfac ne n’estendre l’uef n’autre chose, si com je t’ai fait savoir en la cure de la ramice des intestines;	then pull out the head of the thread, and do not cover the boil or stretch it with anything, as I have instructed you in the treatment of intestinal worms;
puis le cure par la cure des plaies. Et quant tu copes les filz, si le mundefie et cure la plaie, tant qu’elle soit sanee.	then treat it as a wound. And when you tie off the threads, let the boil drain and the wound heal until it is cleaned out.
Li syfac est constrains, et n’a point d’apparance en la routure, et li cauteres est muedres en cest leu, et plus prochiens a salut.	The syphilis is hidden, and has no appearance in the mouth; and the cautery is effective in this place, and is closer to a cure.
de l’amollissement dou cuir des coions	from the softening of the skin of the testicles
Maintes fois est amollis li cuirs des coions en aucuns homes, por ceu que les chars que sont dedens sont mollifiees, et est lait a veoir; et est mestier, quant on le vuet curer, c’on faice gesir lou malaide sus son dos, et li cope le cuir qui est mollifiez sus le cuir natureil; puis assemble les .ij. levres a une costure, et se tu vues, cout premier la superfluiteit dou cuir mollifiiez a .iij. costures ou .iiij. fermement; puis cope entre les costures, et lou cure si com les autres plaies, tant qu’il soit sanez, et chient li fil.	Many times the skin of the testicles becomes soft in some men because the parts inside become soft and look swollen; and when one wants to cure it, he should make the patient lie on his back, and cut the soft skin on top of the natural membrane; then bring together the two lips with a single stitch, or three or four stitches firmly; then cut between the stitches, and treat it like other wounds until it is healed, and remove the stitches.
dou chastrement	from chastity
Saiches que chastremens est escomeniez en nostre loi, et por ceu il me plairoit que je n’en parlasse mie en cest livre; et n’est necessaires fuer que por .ij. manieres: dont l’une est que li mires en saiche respondre quant on li demandera, et en saiche la cure; et li autre, por ceu que nos avons sovent mestier de chastrement d’aucunes bestes por nos aidier, si com de bouc et de mouton et de chait et d’autres bestes. Je dis donques que chastremens est fais selonc .ij. manieres: ou par atraction, ou par fendure.  En celle que nos faisons par attraction, faisons nos seoir la beste en aigue chaude, tant que li coion soient mollifiez et pendant; puis les preing a ta main, tant qu’il soient remis et que tu ne les sentes plus.  Du chastrement de taille: covient que tu teignes la beste, et li presse le cuir des coions a ta main senestre, puis lie le suspensoire, et cope sus chescun oef a .i. cop, quant tu les avras bien escorchiez; et i laisse aucun poc dou syfac et lou subtil syfac qui est sor les vasselz; et ceste maniere de chastrement est muedre que cele qui est faite par attraction, por ceu que a l’atraction demoure par aventure aucune chose des coions, par coi li beste desire luxure; puis cure la plaie tant qu’ele soit sanee.	You know that castration is forbidden by our law, and for that reason I would prefer not to discuss it in this book. However, it is necessary in two cases: the first is so that owners can respond to inquiries about their animals and treat them; the second is because we often need to castrate certain animals to aid us, such as bulls, rams, pigs, and other beasts. Thus, there are two ways of performing castration: either by cutting or by crushing. When we perform it by crushing, we sit the animal in hot water until its testicles become soft and pendant; then we squeeze them with our hand until they are dislodged and we no longer feel anything. As for castration by cutting, one must tie the animal down and press the scrotum against the left hand; then cut it open, applying pressure to each testicle once you have well-scalded them; leave some of the fat and thin membrane that covers the vessels; this method of castration is better than the one performed by crushing, because with crushing something from the testicles may remain, causing the animal to desire sexual intercourse; then treat the wound until it heals.
des hermofrodites	Of hermaphrodites
Hermofrodie est selonc .ij. manieres as homes: l’une si est que entre les .ij. coions apert ausi com li figure de la nature d’une femme, ou il ait poil, et aucunes fois en cort li urine.  Et li autre maniere si est en femmes, et ait sus lou poignil ausi com une verge et .ij. coions.  Et li cure de l’ome et de la fame si est que tu copes les chars ajostees toutes, et les cure si com autres plaies; en la seconde maniere, des homes dont li urine saut par lou cuir des coions, si n’a point de cure.	Hermaphrodites are of two types as men: the first is that between the two testicles appears as the form of nature of a woman, having hair, and sometimes urinate through it. And the other type is in women, having on the scrotum a penis and testicles. And the treatment for both men and women is to cut away the excess flesh, and treat them like any other wound; but for the second type of man, from whom urine escapes through the skin of the testicles, there is no cure.
de la tentigene	of the testicles
Tentigene est une chars ajostee sus la partie natureil, tant qu’elle est trop laide a veoir; et aucunes femmes l’ont ausi grant com une main, et c’est li cure. Il covient que tu teignes la superfluiteit de la tentigene a ta main ou as oncines, et la cope legierement; et n’aler mie trop em parfont, que decorremens de sanc n’i viegne, puis le cure d’autre cure tant qu’il soit sanez; et a une autre char que naist a la bouche de la marris, et l’emple, et par aventure saut fuer, et est selonc la semblance d’une kowe, et por ceu l’apelerent li ancien «maladie kowee». Si covient que tu la copes, si com nos avons dit la tentigene, et la cure tant qu’elle soit sanee.	of the testicles
de erratique	of erratics
Erratique si est quant li nature de la femme n’est mie percie, ou li pertus est petis; et est naturez par naissance, ou accidens par maladie que venue i est; ou c’est par char ajostee, ou dou syfac subtil ou espés, et est fais em parfont en la marris, ou en costez, ou desoz, ou que soit; et deffent le concevoir, et l’enfantement, et par aventure les flors a avoir; et li connoissance de ceu si est par le regart de la baile. Se li estoupemens est prochiens apparans, si quier a tes dois ou au rait. S’il est dou syfac subtil, et il est prochiens as .ij. leivres, si te haste, et la ront ensi: met tes .ij. dois indices ensamble, et li femme soit sus son dos, espandues ses jambes; puis estent les .ij. leivres forment, tant que li subtilz syfac soit rons, et soit overs li estoupemens; puis pren laine, et la moille en oile, et la met sus le leu, et gise li femme a home chescun jor, si qu’il ne puist souder. Et se li syfac est dur et espés, si covient que tu lou copes au spatumile semblant a foille de mirte. Se li estoupemens est de char nee, si la sospent a l’oncine et la cope; et aies les medicines estainchans sanc, si com acaice, sanc de dragon, encens, ensamble abun d’uef; puis amenistre une caine de plonc large, si que li plaie ne puisse souder; et ensi soit longement, et li amenistre une tente de lin sec; puis soit curez d’autres cures tant qu’il soit sanez.  Et quant en la marris vient char nee, si la covient coper selonc ceste maniere, se ce n’est apostemes enchancrez. Car a l’aposteme enchancreit qui est en la marris, ne doit on touchier de feir.	Of erratics: Erratica is a swelling above the natural part, so large and unsightly that it disfigures the patient; some women have them as big as a hand, and this is the cure. You should dye the excess of the tentigene with your fingernails, and scrape gently; do not go too deep, lest bleeding occur, then cure another cure until it heals; and there is another tumor that grows at the mouth of the vagina, use it, and perhaps it will burst, resembling a cow's udder, hence the ancients called it "cow disease." You should treat this as we have said for the tentigene, and cure it until healed.
des emorroides	of hemorrhoids
Emorroydes sont overtures de voines dont sans cort acostumeement, et quant les emorroydes sont vielles si devienent thelul; et nos avons jai dit en la division les semblances d’aus, et les signes, et je dirai ci celles qui resoivent curation. Je di que les emorroides et li thelul, quant il sont em parfont en la marris, et il n’aperent au sentir, si n’est mie li cure par fer. Cil qui sont a la bouche de la marris, c’on puet sentir, sont cil c’on puet curer. Il covient donques que tu mettes la femme en une maison froide, puis estent l’altelul as tenailles, et le cope en ses racines, puis poudre sus medicines restraignans sanc, si com acaice et sanc de dragon et encens, et semblans choses; puis boute ses piez a la paroit une houre, puis la met en aigue froide; et se decorremens de sanc i vient, si la fai seoir en une decoction de sumac et d’escorce de pomes grenates et de gales et de semblans choses, et puis pren farine d’orge, et la confis avec miel et aisil, et en fai .i. emplaustre sus son dos. Et se il estainche, c’est boin. Se ceu non, se li fai aerdre ventouses au dos et as mameles sens ferir; puis pren lainne, et la moille en jus de plantain ou en jus d’aglentier avec vin viel, et fai aerdre au leu.  Et quant li aposteme repose, si cure lou leu d’oignement tant qu’il soit sanez; et celle qui est apelee «albathir» est rouge, et est semblans a .i. chief aspre, si le covient coper si com j’ai dit le thelul; et puis lou cure tant qu’il soit sanez.	Hemorrhoids are opened veins that cause blood to flow, and when hemorrhoids are old, they become throbber; and we have already discussed their likenesses, signs, and treatment methods. I stated that hemorrhoids and throbbers, when they are formed in the anus, and there is no sensation of pain, cannot be cured with a hot iron. Those that form at the mouth of the anus can be sensed and treated. Therefore, one should place the patient in a cool room, then cut off the hemorrhoids with tongs and cauterize their roots with powdered astringent medicines such as acacia, dragon's blood, and incense; then bind her feet to the wall for an hour, and afterwards submerge them in cold water. If there is any bleeding, she should be made to sit in a decoction of sumac, pomegranate peel, galls, and similar substances; and then take barley flour, mix it with honey and garlic, and apply it as a poultice to her back. If the bleeding stops, that is good. If not, leech her back and breasts without using an iron; then take lamb's wool, soak it in plantain juice or dogwood juice mixed with old wine, and apply it to the affected area. Once the abscess has settled, treat the wound with ointment until it heals; and that which is called "albathir" is red and resembles a roughened head, so it should be treated as I have described for throbbers; then cure it until it heals.
des apostemes de la marris	of abscesses in the anus
Maintes manieres d’aposteme vienent en la marris, si com chancre et aposteme pierous et herpes et estiomenes et fistules et emorroides et aposteme chaut, et plusors autres maladies que j’ai dit en la division. Il covient donques que je die en cest traitier l’aposteme chaut qui vient en la marris, qui n’est mie des apostemes que coillent bowe; et se tu vues savoir l’ovraige de fer, si regarde se li apostemes est agus en l’encomencement de sa venue, et plain de chalor et de fievre, et s’il devient rouge se tu le pues veoir.  Adonques ne te haster mie de percier, mais lou fais meurer tant que li dolor soit apaisie; et puis fai seoir lou malaide sus .i. siege, et ait .ij. petis sieges ou il se cline, et apoie sus son dos et assemble ses piez as parties defuer la jambe; et soient ses cuixes espandues, et mette ses braz desoz ses genous, et les lie bien d’un boin liien; puis succe li baille devers lou destre costeit, et i amenistre l’estrument dont on oevre la bouche de la marris, de coi ci aprés vient li forme; et covient que quant tu i vues amenistrer cest estrument, que tu fiches le rait premier ens por savoir la parfondeté de la marris, si que ceu qui entre ens de l’estrument n’i viegne plus em parfont qu’il ne doit, et qu’il ne blece la malaide; et se li estrumens est plus grans, si covient covrir la parfondesce de la marris de drapelz, si que li estrumens ne li grieve; et covient qu’il mette le cornet de l’estrument au desus, et qu’il teigne l’estrument. Et quant li apostemes apert, et on lou fent a la main mol, si le covient coper au chief, au spatumile leit; et quant li bowe est vuidie, si covient que tu mettes en la plaie tentes moillies en oile roset, ou en oile vert sec; et met la tente fuer de la plaie au parfont de la marris, et met par defuer sus la marris et sus le poignil lainne nette moillie en aigue ou malves soient cuites; puis le cure aprés .ij. jors d’oignement avenant a ceu, tant qu’il soit sanez; et aucune fois leve on la marris et la plaie par clistere d’aigue et de miel, et puis d’aigue ou racines de lis et aristologe longe soient cuites; puis reveigne a l’oignement.  Et se li plaie est reponue en la marris, si covient que tu te gardes de cuire de fer, mais cure la si com nos avons dit en la division.	Abscesses in the anus can arise from various causes, such as sores, piercings, herpes, fistulas, hemorrhoids, and hot abscesses, among others, as I have discussed earlier. Now, I will describe the hot abscess that forms in the anus, which is not like those that develop in the bowel. If you want to know how to treat it with iron, observe whether the abscess is painful and red upon its onset, and also consider if there is fever. Then, do not rush to pierce it; instead, let the pain subside first. Next, make the patient sit on a chair, with two small pillows to lean against for support, one on the back and another beneath the feet, which should be spread apart. Place the arms under the knees, and tie them securely with a good cord. Then, suck the anus towards the right side, and insert the instrument used to open the anus, checking the depth of the anus so that the inserted instrument does not go deeper than necessary and cause pain to the patient. If the instrument is larger, cover the depth of the anus with cloth so that it is not irritated. Place the tip of the instrument at the entrance of the anus, and apply pressure while inserting it. When the abscess breaks open and becomes soft, cover the wound with a poultice made from moist rosin or moistened in oil. Place the poultice within the wound, pushing it towards the depth of the anus and over the anus, covering the entire area. Then, apply ointment for two days until the wound heals. Sometimes, raising the anus and cleansing the wound with water and honey helps, followed by applying water in which lily roots and aristolochia have been boiled. Afterwards, return to using the ointment. If the wound has settled within the anus, refrain from using iron; instead, treat it as I have described earlier.
de l’enfantement	of childbirth
Mestier est premier a la baile qu’elle conoisse la figure de l’enfantement natureil, et li signes si est quant tu vois la femme apresser aval, et desire odorer l’ar: adonques se haste li enfes de fuer issir; adonc saiches que cil enfantemens est selonc la figure natureil, et est li issue soz son chief, et li secondine avec lui; et quant tu vois ces signes, si covient presser legierement son ventre, si que li enfes isse tost; car quant il dessent sus son chief, si ist li secondine avec lui, et est mondee li marris de ses superfluitez par bone mundification; et cist qui vient autrement ne vient mie naturelment. Car il vient aucune fois sus ses piez, et vient fuer li cors ou li chiés, et les mains, ou il vient sus son ventre, ou sovin, et est convertis par aventure sor son col, et par autres figures malvaises; si est mestier a la baile qu’elle soit saige et subtilz en ces choses, et se warse d’error et de decevement, et je vos mostrerai toutes les figures coment on li doit aidier.	It is necessary for the midwife to first understand the natural process of childbirth and its signs; when you see the woman pushing downward and desiring to smell aromatic herbs, then hasten the child's delivery; then you will know that this childbirth follows nature's course, and the baby emerges head first, followed by the بعدين with it; and when you see these signs, gently press her abdomen so that the baby is delivered promptly; for when the baby descends toward the head, the afterbirth comes with it, and the mother's excess fluids are expelled through proper cleansing; and anything different from this is not a natural birth. Sometimes the baby emerges feet first, or the body or shoulder, hands, or abdomen, and in some cases, the baby may be turned upside down; there are many unnatural positions. Thus, the midwife must be wise and astute in these matters, guarding against error and deception, and I shall explain to you how to assist in all these various scenarios.
Se li enfes vient sus son chief par issue natureil, et li femme enfante griement, et li vertus de li est foible, si la fai seoir sus une selle, ou les femmes la tienent; et arose sa nature d’oile ou fenugreic soit cuit, et puis boute li baile entre ses dois le petit spatumile dont ci est li forme:	If the baby emerges head first in a natural delivery, and the woman gives birth with great effort due to her weak constitution, then make her sit on a stool or have other women support her; then apply a warm ointment made from fried oil or fenugreek between the midwife's fingers in the form of a small spatula:
et fende la secondine, et cope a son ungle tant que li moistors qui est ens corre fuers; et preint lou ventre de la femme tant que li enfes dessende, et s’il ne dessent, si covient clisterizer la femme de muscillaige de fenugrec avec oile de sisament; puis la fai preindre et esternuer de condisi, et tien sa bouche et son neis une houre: si istra maintenant l’enfes.Et se les .ij. mains issent fuer, si covient que tu les ramoinne legierement poc et poc; et s’elles n’i puent entrer, si met la femme sus .i. siege, et li lieve les piés en haut; puis deboute le siege sus terre, et teigne on la femme, qu’elle ne chiece au deboutement; et se li mains n’i puet entrer, et li enfes muert, si li cope les mains au couteil qui est ci devant mis, et estrai l’enfant, et ramoine igalment.	and split the afterbirth, and scrape its edges until the moistness that is within flows out; then pinch the woman's abdomen so that the baby descends, and if it does not descend, give her a clyster made from fenugreek with warming oil; then make her sneeze and cough gently, and hold her mouth and nose for an hour; then the baby will be delivered. And if both hands emerge first, then gently push them back in little by little; and if they cannot go back in, have the woman sit on a chair and lift her feet up; then stand the chair on the ground and rock it slightly so that she leans forward; and if the hands still cannot go back in, and the baby is dead, then grab the hands at the knuckles as described earlier, extract the child, and proceed likewise.
de l’issue de l’enfant sus ses piez	of the delivery of the child on its feet
Quant li enfes vient sus ses piez, si lou covient bouter en haut;	When the child comes out on its feet, it should be turned upside down.
et puis le torne poc et poc, tant qu’il soit igalz;	And then turn it slowly, until it is straightened out;
puis preigne .i. des piez et l’estende poc et poc.	then grab one of the feet and stretch it out slowly.
Cant il saut jusc’as cuixes, si la comande a preindre, et la fai esternuer de condisi;	When it jumps up to the armpit, instruct him to grab it, and make him sneeze forcefully;
si saut fuer, se Deus vuet.	if he jumps out, God willing.
Et s’il n’ist fuer si com nos avons dit, si le torne poc et poc, tant qu’il soit selonc la figure natureil.	And if it doesn't jump out as we have said, then slowly turn it back to its natural position.
Car adonques ist il legierement.	For then it is easy.
Et s’il ne vient fuer si com nos avons dit, si pren muscillaige de altee, et oile de sisament, et gomme fondue, et broie tout en .i. mortier;	And if it does not work as we have said, take myrrh, and oil of six-year-old wine, and melted gum, and grind everything in a mortar;
et met sus la nature de la femme dedens et defuer cest oignement,	and put it on the woman's nature inside and let this ointment work,
puis la fai seoir en aigue tede jusque desoz les costelz;	then let her sit in warm water up to her ribs;
et quant elle est moillifie desoz, se li fai .i. coliere de mirre, et li met desoz, et li laisse une houre;	and when she is softened underneath, make a collar of myrrh for her, and put it on her underneath, and leave it for an hour;
puis la fai seoir sus .i. siege, puis la fai esternuer et estraint sa bouche et son neis, et li preint le ventre legierement, car li enfes saut maintenant.	then make her sit on a chair, then make her sneeze and hold her mouth and nose shut, and gently press her belly, for the child will come out soon.
de l’issue de l’enfant sus ses genous	the child will emerge onto its knees
Quant li enfes vient en ceste forme, si i mette li baile ses mains poc et poc;	When the child comes in this form, then you must gently place your hands on it;
puis soit sovinee sus son col, et li pendent li piez aval, et soit gisans sor .i. lit;	then let him be laid on his back, and let his feet hang down, and let him lie on a bed;
et plie ses mains poc et poc, et puis li preint les mains sus lou ventre, et li oste les cussins desoz, tant qu’elle soit appareillie aval;	and folds his hands a little, and then he presses his hands on his belly, and takes the cushions from under him, so that she is prepared below;
et se li enfes ne saut, si pren ses piez et li muef forment, puis li muef lou ventre amont, puis i boute tes mains;	and if the child does not jump, then take his feet and move them about, then move his belly upwards, then push with your hands;
et ewe l’enfant poc et poc; et comande a la femme qu’elle se preigne tant que li enfes isse.	and rock the child gently; and instruct the woman to hold on until the child emerges.
de l’issue de l’enfant qui vient dou large une main pendant	of the emergence of the child who comes out with one hand hanging down
I covient engignier a ramener la main:	It is necessary to know how to replace the hand:
s’on ne la puet ramener, si fai lever la femme, et aler;	if it cannot be replaced, then make the woman stand up and walk;
s’elle ne puet aler, si la fai gesir sus .i. lit, et li deboute les jambes forment;	if she cannot walk, then make her lie on a bed and raise her legs straight;
puis amenistre lou muscillaige que j’ai conteit;	then apply the medicine that I have described;
et s’elle n’enfante, si la fai seoir sus .i. siege, puis estudie au rameneir la main;	and if she does not give birth, then make her sit on a chair, and then try to bring the hand back;
et ewe l’enfant selonc la figure natureil, et la fai esternuer, et li comande qu’elle se preigne tant que li enfes isse fuer.	and turn the child according to its natural position, and make her sneeze, and command that she squeeze until the baby comes out.
de l’issue de l’enfant sus son col, et ait espandues ses mains, et sa faice tornee devers lou dos sa mere	from the child's exit above its neck, and spread her hands, and turn her face towards her mother's back
I covient que li baile teigne sa main, puis le torne poc et poc, et l’ewe legierement;	I must make him grip her hand, then turn it slowly, and gently;
et quant il est igalz, si met sus la nature muscillaige de altee et oile, si com nos avons dit, puis li comande qu’elle se mueve poc et poc;	and when it is even, then put on the nature of mustard and oil, as we have said, then instruct that it moves a little bit at a time.
et quant tu avras ce fait, si la fai seoir sus .i. siege, et li comande k’elle se preigne; et la fai esternuer.	and when you have done this, then make her sit on a seat, and instruct her to sneeze; and make her yawn.
de ceste meisme maniere a tout la secondine	in the same way for all the afterbirth
Quant il vient fuer en ceste maniere a tout la secondine, si cope la secondine a ton ungle, tant que li moistors soit vuidie;	When it comes out in this way to all the afterbirth, then grip the afterbirth with your finger, as long as the moisture is emptied;
et se li enfes pent sus sa faice et sus son col, si la cope des la boude, qu’elle ne soit retenue, et muere li enfes;	and if the child puts its hands on its face and neck, and the mother slaps it so that it is not restrained, and the child dies;
puis boute l’enfant dedens, tant que tu l’aies mis si com il covient, et comande a la femme qu’elle se preigne aucune fois:	then put the child inside, as you should, and instruct the woman to hold on for a while;
adonques si istra legierement.	then if it is released easily.
de l’issue des gemelz	of the hernia
Saiches que gemeil naissent maintes fois, et aucune fois en naissent .iij. ou .iiij.; et ceu n’est mie estrainge chose, et poc avient.	Know that twins are born many times, and sometimes three or four; and this is not a strange thing, but it happens rarely.
Dui sont estrainge chose, et ne vivent mie, se poc nom;	[I think there is a mistake here as the previous sentence ends with "and it happens rarely", so I will assume there was meant to be a 'but' instead of 'poc' in this line.]
je sai ceu, qu’il soient multipliiet, et sont desevrez par lou syfac qui les devise, qui est liiez a la boude;	I know that they are split [or divided], and are separated by the sac that divides them, which is attached to the placenta.
et aucune fois issent ausi naturelment com uns tous sous, si com nos avons dit.	and sometimes they issue just as naturally as a single child, as we have said.
Et s’il issent griement, si la cure si com nos avons dit, et soit li baile subtilz, et faice tost et legierement ceu qu’elle fait;	And if they are bleeding heavily, then apply the treatment as we have said, and let the bandages be fine, and quickly and gently do what she does.
et faice ensi com il vaut mues a salut.	and do thus whatever will bring about healing.
de plusors enfans	of many children
Aucune fois sont formez en la marris .i. ou .ij. ou .iij. ou .iiij. ou .v. ou .vj. ou .vij., ou plusors jusc’a .xv., et sont tout formeit en forme d’enfant par le mesurement dou saige glorious,	Sometimes they are formed in the womb as one, or two, or three, or four, or five, or six, or seven, or more, up to fifteen, and they are all formed in the shape of a child according to the measurement of the glorious sage,
et couvient que li baile saiche tout ceu, car par aventure semblans chose li avient;	and one must teach the patient everything, for by chance something like this may happen to him;
si faice selonc ceu qu’il covient.	then act according to what is appropriate.
de l’enfant mort	of a dead child
Quant tu cures la femme de l’enfant mort ou ventre, si com j’ai dit en la division, et il ne vient fuers, et tu es constrains d’ovraige de mains;	When you are treating a woman for a dead fetus or pregnancy, as I have said in the previous section, and there is no progress, and you are forced to use manual methods;
si covient que tu saiches se li femme est de saine vertut, et n’ait accident ou elle ait paor de mort;	if you should know whether the woman is of sound body, and has no fear of death.
si covient que li femme soit sovinee sus son dos, et soit ses chiés enclins aval, et les jambes levees;	the woman should be laid on her back, with her hips tilted down, and her legs raised;
et li ministre la teigne de .ij. pars, ou elle soit liie au lit si qu’elle ne soit traite au dessendement de l’enfant;	and the midwife should apply a compress of ten parts, binding it to her abdomen so that she is not treated for the descent of the child;
puis frotez la bouche de la marris d’oiles moistes avec muscillaige de altee et de fenugrec et semence de lin, puis oigne li baile ses mains de ces oiles et de ces muscillaiges;	then rub the mouth of the mother with moist oils infused with myrrh and fenugreek and flax seed, then anoint the midwife's hands with these oils and myrrh;
puis les boute en la marris legierement, puis quiere .i. leu ou elle boute les oncines que soient covenaubles a ceu,	then gently tap them, then put them in a place where they can grow,
et pren warde se li enfes est apparilliez qu’il dessende sus son chief;	and take care that the baby does not fall on its head;
si fiche les oncines en ses eulz ou en son col ou en sa bouche ou en som palais ou desoz la barbe ou en la forcele ou pres des costez,	if it sticks the nails in its eyes or nose or mouth or throat or beard or armpit or near the ribs,
et se li dessendemens est sus piez, se li fiche ou poignil et as costes moienes;	and if the swelling is on the feet, then stab it or pinch it at the middle of the shins;
et covient qu’il teigne l’oncine a sa main destre, et mette la corbeure entre ses dois de la senestre main, et li boute a tout sa main legierement, et fiche l’oncine en aucun de ces leus que nos avons dit, tant qu’il viegne a la chose vuide;	and he should dye the nail on his right hand, and place the thread between the fingers of his left hand, and wind it around his whole hand gently, and insert the needle into one of the places we have mentioned, until it reaches the hollow space;
et c’est li forme de l’oncine:	and this is how the needle should be shaped:
puis fiche encontre .i. autre oncine, ou le tier se tu en as mestier, si que li estractions soit igalz;	then pierce with another needle, or a third one if you need it, so that the extractions are equal;
et puis l’estent igalment en movant d’une part et d’autre, por mues issir, et soit li oncines dentez por mues tenir, si com ci est li forme:	and then they should be equally tight by moving from one side to another so that the movement can happen, and the needles should be bitten down upon so as to hold the movement in place, as shown here in this illustration:
Et s’il en demoure une partie, si oigne li baile aucuns de ses dois d’oile, et les boute en celle partie, et traie l’autre partie;	And if a portion remains, then anoint one of his fingers with oil, and rub it into that part, and draw the other part.
et s’il en i demoure point, si met cest oncine ou plus haut leu, et fai ceu tant qu’il s’en isse tout fuers.	and if nothing remains, then put this joint or a higher one in place, and hold it until all the strength goes out.
Et se l’une mains vient devant l’autre, et il ne puet ramener por l’estreignement,	And if one hand comes before the other, and he cannot pull back due to the dislocation,
si covient que tu envoloupes sus .i. drapeil, tant qu’il isse tote;	then you must wrap it with a cloth, until it all comes out.
puis la cope en la jointure de la plante ou au coute, et ensi covient que tu faices en l’autre main, et as .ij. piés.	then the scald on the bend of the foot or on the elbow, and likewise you should do to the other hand and both feet.
Et se li chiés de l’enfant est gros et il est estrois en l’issue, ou il ait ou chief aigue assemblee,	And if the child's head is big and it is constricted in the birth canal, or it has acute pain concentrated in one spot,
si covient que tu boute le spatumile espinous entre tes dois, et fent le chief et estrai l’aigue;	you should insert a thorn between your fingers, and pierce the head to draw out the venom.
ou tu la ront a l’estrument qui est apelez «almidach», de coi li forme vient avec les estrumens ou chapistre qui est aprés cestui;	or you can use the instrument called "almidach", whose shape comes from the instrument in this chapter.
et ensi meisme faice se li enfes a grant chief naturelment;	and thus the child is born with a large head naturally;
et puis traie fuer les osses as tenailles,	and then pulls out the bones with tongs,
et se li chiés saut fuer et il estraint a la forcele, si soit fendus, tant que li moistors qui est ou pis issue fuer;	and if the shoulder pops out and is forced back in, it should be split open so that the moisture which is causing the problem can escape;
et s’elle ne puet issir, si le cope par pieces au mues que tu pues;	and if it cannot come out, then cut it into pieces as much as you can;
et s’il est enflez au ventre ou desoz les costez, si covient que tu lou perces tant que li moistors corre.	and if it is swollen in the belly or under the ribs, you must pierce it so that the moisture runs out.
Et se li enfes est sus ses piez, si est li attraction legiere, et li adrecemens a la bouche de la marris est legier.	And if the swelling is on his feet, the pull is light, and the movement towards the mouth of the wound is easy.
Et s’il est estrois au ventre ou au pis, si couvient que tu l’estraies a .i. drapeil envoloupeit sus la main;	And if it is tight in the belly or the foot, you must stretch it with one folded cloth wrapped around your hand;
et fent le ventre ou le pis, tant que li moistors qui i est corre;	and open the belly or the foot, so that the moisture which is in there runs out;
et se li autre membre sont osteit, et li chiez demoure,	and if the other members are removed, and the head remains,
si boute li baile sa main em parfont de la marris, et le traie jusc’a la bouche de la marris;	then he should put his hand into the wound and pull it out to the mouth of the wound;
puis i boute .i. oncine ou ij., et le trai fuer;	then he should cut off one or two nails, and draw it out;
et se li bouche de la marris est retrecie por aposteme chaut qui i est venus, si n’i covient mie travillier,	and if the mouth of the wound is narrowed by a hot abscess that has formed there, one should not work on it,
ains covient amenistrer choses moistes et grasses;	one must administer moist and fatty things;
et li amenistre emplaustres, et siece en aigue mollifians et amoistans.	and one should apply poultices, and use warm water that softens and moistens.
Et se li enfes est sus son costeit, et tu le pues mettre igal, si amenistre ceu que nos avons dit en l’enfant vif;	And if the child is on its side, and you can get it to lie down flat, then administer what we have said for a living child:
et s’on nen ait pooir, si lou trai fuer par pieces, et n’i laissier rien de la secondine.	and if one cannot, then carry the child out by pieces, and leave nothing of the placenta behind.
Et quant tu avras ce fait, se li amenistre ceu que nos avons dit ens apostemes chaus que vienent en la marris;	And when you have done this, if he is affected with those abscesses that come in the sea;
et se decorremens de sanc vient, si soit mise en aigue restraignant, et li amenistre autres cures.	and blood flows out, let it be put into cold water, and let other remedies be applied.
Et je vis une femme en cui ventre uns enfes avoit esteit mors, puis consut .i. autre sus celui, et refut mors li autres.	And I saw a woman in whose belly some fetus had been dead, then another was sewn over it, and the other died as well.
Aprés lonc tens li vint uns apostemes en la boude, et enfla tant qu’il ovrit, et comensa a grant porreture.	After a long time, an abscess came in her armpit, and swelled so much that it opened, and began to discharge profusely.
je fui apelez a la cure, et i pensai lonc tens, et ne pot soder li plaie.	I was called to the priest, and I thought for a long time, and could not heal the wound.
Je mis sus emplaustre de fort attraction, et en issit uns os, et aprés aucuns jors uns autres.	I applied a strong attractive plaster, and an bone came out, and after a few days another one did too.
Je me mervillai mout, por ceu c’ou ventre n’a point d’os.	I was very surprised because the belly has no bones.
Si pensai que c’estoit des os d’un enfant mort.	I thought they were the bones of a dead child.
Je quis la plaie, et en traï mains os, tant que li femme fut em miglior point;	Examine the wound, and use your hands to feel for bones, until the woman is in a better state.
et vesquit li femme lonc tens ensi, et issoit adés un poc de bowe dou leu;	and let the woman stay like this for a long time, and then move her bowels slightly from her position;
et je n’ai recordeit cest chapistre fuer que por ceu que, quant li maistres trueve une estrainge chose, qu’il i saiche mettre aide.	and I have included this chapter only because when the master finds something unusual, he can apply a remedy.
dou ramener la marris a son leu	to bring the dislocation back to its place
Ci aprés vient li forme dou pressor, a coi on ewe les livres; et a .ij. tornans as .ij. chiés des .ij. liiens.	Hereafter comes the form of the press, to which one ties books; and at two turns of the two arms.
Toutevoie, li cornes soit plus subtilz dou restrictoire, et soit fais de ebene ou de bux;	Nevertheless, let the horns be more subtle than the constrictor, and made of boxwood or ebony;
et soit li bouche dou fust .i. doi de large, et li marge des arbres .i. doit, et de lonc une palme et demi;	and let the mouth of the beam be one digit wide, and the edges of the wood one digit apart, and one palm and a half long;
et enmi les .ij. liemens soient dui ajostemens de cest meisme fust, qui soient fermeit en l’un et en l’autre, de demi palme de lonc ou un poc plus;	and in the two beams are two adjustments of this same beam, which are fastened in one and the other, half a palm long or a little more;
et cist dui ajostement sont bouteit en la bouche de la marris por ovrir quant on torne les .ij. cornes.	and these two adjustments are put into the mouth of the wound to open when you turn the two horns.
Une autre forme, a sa semblance plus subtilz et plus legiere, soit faite de fust de ebene ou de bux, selonc la semblance des tenailles;	Another form, more subtle and lighter in appearance, is made of ivory or boxwood, according to the likeness of tweezers;
et ait as .ij. chiés .ij. ajostemens, si com tu vois, d’une palme de lonc, et .ij. dois de large;	and has two ends with two adjustments, as you see, a palm long and two fingers wide;
et quant tu vues ovrir la marris a tout l’estrument, si fai seoir la femme sor .i. lit, les piez pendant et les jambes overtes,	and when you see to open the wound with all the instrument, then let the woman sit on a bed, her feet hanging and her legs spread,
puis boute les .ij. ajostemens ajostez ensamble en la marris, et tien le chief de l’estrument desoz entre ses cuixes;	then put the two pieces of the instrument together in the water, and hold the head of the instrument under between his thighs;
puis oevre ta main a tout l’estrument, si com tu as fait as tenailles igalment, selonc la quantiteit que tu vues ovrir la bouche de la marris, tant que li baile faice ceu qu’elle vuet.	then work your hand on the instrument, just like you did with the pliers, according to how much you want to open the mouth of the water, as long as the patient does what he wants.
Cist estrument sont tuit sormontez, et sont multiplies lor semblances; et quant li mires les ait apareilliez, tant est plus hastans li oevre, et plus haute as homes por lor quantiteit.	These instruments are all decorated, and their designs vary; and when the patient sees them prepared, the effect is more immediate and more powerful on people due to their appearance.
Si ne despire mie l’estrument que tu ne l’aies apparelliet, car lor necessitez n’est mie escusauble.	Do not be discouraged by the instrument until you have prepared it, for their needs are not preventable.
Quant li secondine est retenue a l’enfantement, si covient que tu comandes a la malaide qu’ele reteigne son alaine, et puis la fai esternuer de condisi, et li estraint tes mains a la bouche et au neis;	When the placenta is retained after childbirth, you must instruct the patient to hold in her breath and then make her sneeze with an aromatic substance. You must then press her hands against her mouth and nose.
et s’elle saut per ceu, bien est.	And if she urinates through it, that is good.
Se ceu non, si prent .i. pot, et fai .i. pertus ou cuvercle, et i met herbes que puissent ovrir la bouche de la marris, si com calament, rue, anis, camomille, cassialigne et centoire;	If not, take a container and make an opening in its cover, and place herbs that can open the mouth of the womb, such as hellebore, rue, anise, chamomile, casia, and centaury.
toutes ces herbes, ou aucunes d’eles, soient cuites ou pot en aigue sus le feu; puis met une caine ou pertus dou pot, et l’autre chief en la bouche de la marris,	All these herbs, or some of them, are cooked in water over fire. Then place one end of the straw into the opening of the pot and the other end into the mouth of the womb,
et la teigne tant que li vapors viegne dedens la marris; puis la fai esternuer, si com nos avons dit.	and the dye until the vapors enter the marble; then make it sneeze, as we have said.
Si saut li secondine hastanment.	Then the secondine suddenly.
Et s’elle remaint aprés ceste cure, et n’ist mie fuer, si comande a la baile qu’ele moille sa main senestre en oile de sesement ou en muscillaige de altee, et puis la boute en la nature,	And if it remains after this treatment, and is not better, order the bather to moisten her left hand in oil of sesame or in musk-balm, and then put it back in the natural position,
et quiere la secondine; et quant elle l’avra trovee, si la preigne et l’estende poc et poc droitement, si que li marris ne chiece a l’estraction;	and desire the secondine; and when she has found it, she should squeeze it and stretch it little by little straight, so that the marble does not crack;
mais la covient movoir legierement a destre et a senestre, et puis traie; si venra et se desaerdra.	But it must be moved slightly to the right and left, and then pulled; thus it will come loose and release itself.
Et se li bouche de la marris est jai estrecie, nos avons dit la cure d’esternuer, et de fumigation des herbes;	And if the opening of the wound is tight, we have discussed the cure for sneezing and the fumigation of herbs;
et s’elle n’ist de tout ceu que nos avons dit, si garde que tu ne foloies au traire;	and if it is not from anything that we have mentioned, then be careful not to pull;
mais il couvient que ceu qui est a la bouche de la marris, que tu le lies a la cuixe de la femme, puis la clisterize d’oignement tetrafarmaçon;	but it is necessary that he who is at the mouth of the wound tie it to the woman's thigh, then cleanse her with a four-drug ointment;
si la porrira et remettra, et venra fuer; mais toutevoie, quant elle porrist si en vient male odor au stomac et au chief, et blece la malaide.	if she vomits and it comes out, but nonetheless, when she vomits, there is a bad smell in the stomach and head, and it weakens the sick person.
Si covient donques fumigations covenaubles a ceu: aucun des anciens ont esproveit fumigation de cresson et de figues seches.	If necessary, therefore, appropriate fumigations should be used: some of the ancients have tried fumigation with watercress and dried figs.
Li forme de l’estrument a coi on fumige la femme a la retenue des flors et de la secondine si est ceste:	The shape of the instrument with which one smokes out the woman for the retention of flowers and afterbirth, if it is this:
Et est de voirre semblant a une caine, et met on le chief subtil en la nature, et les chiés larges sus le feu;	And it is made of glass like a cane, and one puts the pointed end into the nature, and the wide ends above the fire;
et soit li fumigations sus les charbons, et la teigne tant qu’elle soit gastee, et rencomence une autre.	and let there be fumigation over the coals, and the tinder until it is wasted, and begin another.
de percier lou fondement	of piercing the foundation
Maint enfant naissent qui n’ont mie le fondement perciet, ains l’ait estoupeit uns subtilz syfac:	Many children are born who do not have their foundation pierced, but rather have a subtle hymen:
si covient donques a la baile qu’ele perce celui syfac a son doit, et ne lou perce mie de spatumile agut, et garse le lacement qu’elle ne le touche;	so it is necessary for the midwife to pierce the hymen with her finger, and not with a pointed instrument, and to be careful that she does not tear it;
puis met sus lainne moillie en vin et en oile, puis la cure d’oignement tant qu’il soit sanez.	then place on a wet cloth with wine and oil, then treat the wound with ointment until it heals.
Et se tu doutes qu’il ne restoupe, si met ou pertus une caine de plonc, et li laisse mains jors, et soit ostee quant li enfes vuet aler en chambres.	And if you doubt that it will heal, then put a splint of wood through the wound, and leave it for several days, and remove it when the child wants to walk.
Et aucune fois vient cist estoupemens de soudement de plaie ou d’aposteme; si covient coper celui soudement: si soit curez, si com nos avons dit de la caine de plonc.	And sometimes this healing happens suddenly from a wound or abscess; then it must be covered suddenly: it should be treated, as we have said, with a splint of wood.
de la fistule dou fondement	from the fistula in the anus
Fistules qui vienent desoz le fondement sont nodation, et groissor que vienent delez lou fondement defuer, ou en l’espaice des .ij. parties,	Fistulas that come from under the anus are nodular and grow larger than those that come from the anus itself or in the space between its two halves.
si a une fistule ou plusors; et quant celle nodation est anciene, si aoeuvre, et encort moistor awouse blainche ou subtilz bowe,	If there is one or more fistula; and when that nodule is old, it opens and secretes a white moisture or thin pus,
et aucune fois sont ces fistule persans; et sont conues par ceu qu’il en ist ou egestion ou ventositeit quant li malaide fait egestion, et par aventure en saut uns vers.	and sometimes these fistulas are perforated; and they are caused by what comes out of the anus or by flatulence when the patient breaks wind, and occasionally one of them pops out.
Et si a fistules que percent jusc’a la vessie, et jusc’a la moitiet de la verge; et parvienent jusc’a la jointure de la cuixe, et jusc’a nout de la kowe.	And there are fistulas that pierce all the way to the bladder, and halfway down the penis; and they reach up to the hip joint, and even to the testicles.
Et ensi conoist on la fistule persant au fondement, et ne mie persant:	And so one recognizes the fistula when it is persistent in the anus, but not persisting.
et est que tu boutes ton doi indice ou fondement, et boute une aguille subtil d’arain ou de fer en la fistule quant il n’i a tortuositeit.	and you put your index finger or thumb into the anus and push a thin needle made of bronze or iron into the fistula when there is no twisting.
Et s’il ait tortuositeit, si i boute une tente de plonc subtil, ou .i. poil de cheval, tant que tu sentes la tente ou le poil a ton doit;	And if it has a twist to it, then you insert a slender probe made of lead or a horsehair until you feel the probe or hair at your finger;
et se tu ne le sens, et il ne vient dou pertus egestion ne ventositeit ne ver, si com nos avons dit:	and if you do not feel it, and there is no pus or wind coming out, as we have said:
saiches qu’elle ne perce mie; si te haste dou curer.	know that it does not pierce; then hurry to heal it.
Et quant li fistule est persans jusc’a la vessie ou jusc’a conduit de l’urine, si en saut li urine, et ne puet soudeir par medicines.	And when the fistula extends to the bladder or the urethra, and the urine leaks out, and cannot be stopped by medicine.
S’elle est percie jusc’a la jointure de la cuixe, si est li tente venans jusc’au leu;	If it is pierced up to the hip joint, then the tent is pushed up to the site.
s’il n’i a tortuositeit et li invention de la dolor entor, si est qu’il en ist adés bowe, et n’i vaut medicine ne soudement par oignement;	If there is twisting and pain in the groin, then it is that it must be cut out, and medicine or ointment will not help.
et en ces fistules persans n’a point de cure fuer que labor, et vaniteit des folz mires qui s’en entremettent.	and for these persistent ulcers there is no cure despite the effort and the foolish remedies of those who interfere.
En celle qui n’est mie persans et n’est mie anciene, a esperance de saniteit par fer, si com j’ai esproveit,	For one that is not persistent and is not old, there is hope of healing by iron, as I have experienced.
et est que li malaides gise entre tes mains sus son dos; et li lieve les jambes jusque sus ses cuixes, et ait ses cuixes enclinees a son ventre;	And let the patient lie on his back, and raise his legs up to his thighs, and have his thighs tilted towards his belly;
puis boute une tente d’arain, ou de plonc s’il i a tortuositeit, tant que tu saiches ou li tente vient.	then insert a tent of iron, or of wood if there is twisting, as much as you know where the tent comes from.
Se li malaides la sent entor le fondement, si covient que tu i boutes ton doi indice,	If the patient feels pain around their anus, you must insert your index finger.
se sens adonques que li tente l’ait perciet; et soit descoverte ou tu sens entre ton doit le syfac ou la char, adonques saiches qu’elle est persans;	If you then feel that it pierces the rectum; and whether it is uncovered where you feel between your finger the anus or the flesh, then know that it is perforated;
si n’i travillier mie c’on ne la puet saner.	if one does not work on it, it cannot be healed.
On dist toutevoie c’on em puet bien saner aucuns, mais ce avient poc;	One says nevertheless that some can be healed well, but that happens rarely;
et li aide c’on i fait, si est c’on eschaufe le cautere subtil selonc la largesce de la fistule, si com il est devant dit;	and the aid which is done, one burns the cautery sutilly according to the width of the fistula, as it was said before;
et le boute tout chaut en la fistule, tant qu’il viegne delez le fondement; et faice ceu .ij. fois ou .iij., tant que tu saiches que ces chars fautrees soient arses, qui sont semblant a une penne d’oiseil;	and put it all hot into the fistula, as far as the anus; and do this twice or thrice, until you know that these burnt threads are burnt, which look like a feather of a bird;
et puis le cure de tentes moillies em burre, tant que celle chars isse fuer, puis le cure d’oignement enjanrant char et soudant.	and then treat it with moist bandages soaked in butter, until the threads come out, and then treat it with ointment to heal and close the wound.
S’il est ensi sanez, c’est bien. Se ceu, nom autrement ne puet estre sanez;	If it is thus healed, that is good. If not, it cannot be healed otherwise;
et se li tente entre, et ne perce jusc’au doit qui est ou fondement, et a entre ton doi et la tente une coverture espesse de char ou de syfac, et tu vois la fistule a ceu qui enseut la coverture dou keur;	and if the tent is inserted and does not penetrate to the depth that is at the foundation, and there is between your finger and the tent a thick covering of flesh or of syphac, and you see the fistula in that which follows the covering of the heart;
si le cope des l’encomencement de la fistule, et boute adés avant la tente, et pues le cautere aprés, tant qu’il viegne au chief de la tente;	if you cut at the beginning of the fistula, and then plug it before the tent, and then cauterize afterwards, until it reaches the head of the tent;
et sera delivré li tente, et cherra; puis mondefie celles chars fautrees que semblent une penne d’oisel, et n’en remaigne niant.	and the tent will be delivered, and will fall out; then cut off those falsified flesh that looks like a bird's feather, and nothing will remain.
Et si li sans te vaint, et cort entre toi et l’uevre, si le cauterize de feu ou de medicine ague.	And if the pus runs out, and flows between you and the wound, then cauterize it with fire or with medicine.
Car li cauteres de feu assemble .ij. bones choses: c’est a savoir, l’arsure de ces chars ajostees, et l’esteinchement de sanc et la sechor de la moistor;	For fire cautery brings together two things: scorching of the flesh and bloodletting, and drying out moisture;
puis le cure de tentes moillies em burre ou en choz broiez, tant que li leus giete bowe, et isse fuer li chars arse en la bowe;	then tent treatment with butter or crushed substances, until the pus flows out and the burns heal.
puis cure la plaie des oignemens soudans enjanrans dure char, et sont les medicines seches.	then treat the wound with poultices of soft, moist, black, charred matter; and the remedies are dry.
Car quant il est restoree, si est sanee et ne revient mie.	For when it is restored, it is healed and does not return.
Et se fistule vient jusc’a parfont dou fondement, et est esloigniez dou cors, se li boute ton doi ou fondement, et enquier ceu.	And if a fistula comes all the way from the anus, and is separated from the body, put your finger in it or plug it up, and ask for help.
Se tu sens la tente, et entre .ij. est li toile ou li syfac ou chars, ou il est pres a percier, si n’i ait fuers que voie de fiance et d’esperance, par l’aministrement de l’une des .iii. manieres:	If you feel the hernia, and between them is the testicle or scrotum, or it is ready to rupture, then do not delay but seek treatment immediately using one of three methods:
ou tu le cauterizes si com nos avons dit, ou tu le cope jusc’a fons, ou se tu pues si i met tentes et cure si com premier;	either by cauterizing it as we have said, or cutting it to the bottom, or if you can, insert a tent and treat it as before.
et n’aler mie trop em parfont, que tu ne coper le tenement qui tient le fondement, et viegne li egestions par lai sens volenteit;	And do not go too deep, lest you cut into the bowel that holds the anus and cause an erection through which waste may exit.
puis le cure, si com nos avons dit;	then treat, as we have said;
par aventure si sera sanez, ou tu esloigne celle coverture et la munde puis qu’elle est copee delez lou fondement, ou par tente ou par autre estrument apointé;	by chance you will be cured, or remove that covering and clean it after it has been cut away from the foundation, or by tent or by another pointed instrument;
puis mondefie cele char fautree qui est en la plaie, tant com tu pues;	then probe the wound, as much as you can;
puis estudie a restorer la plaie, et a demorer la fistule en la partie defuers le fondement: si iert plus legiere chose au malaide.	then examine how to restore the wound and keep the fistula in the part above the foundation: if it is a lighter thing for the patient.
Et aucune fois sont fistules selonc ceste maniere: et est quant tu boutes la tente en la fistule, et elle est ou costeit dou fondement delez lou cuir desus,	And sometimes they are fistulas according to this way: it is when you put the tent in the fistula and it is at the side of the foundation next to the skin above.
si pren une tente percie au chief selonc ceste forme:	Take a tent pierced at the top according to this form:
Et i boute .i. fil tort en .ij., et boute la tente a tout le fil en la fistule tant qu’il soit au chief.	And thread .ii. threads through it, and push the tent all the way through the fistula until it reaches the top.
S’elle est persans en la marge dou fondement dedens, adonc estrai lou fil de celui pertus, ensi que tu boutes ton doi ou fondement;	If it pierces through the margin within the foundation, then pull out the thread from that opening, so that you push your finger into the foundation;
et trai le chief dou fil, et assemble les .ij. chiés ensamble, et estraint l’un a l’autre, et le laisse .i. jor ou .ij.;	and draw the head with thread, and bring together the two heads together, and hold one to the other, and leave them for one or two days;
et le restraint aucune fois, tant que li filz cope ces chars que sont entre dous, et chiecent;	and restrain it sometimes, until the threads cut through the flesh that is between them, and separate;
puis cure la plaie tant qu’elle soit soudee et sanee.	then cure the wound until it is healed and clean.
Se li fistule ne perce, si la fai percier en toutes les manieres que tu pues, s’ele n’est trop em parfont.	If the fistula does not burst, then have it burst in every way you can, if it is not too deep.
