Car il ne covient mie faire por le lacement coper si em parfont, et puis le cure, si com nos avons dit, tant qu’il soit sanez.	Because it is not appropriate to bandage too tightly and then to treat, as we have said, until it has healed.
Li forme dou spatumile espinous dont on fent la fistule si est mout agus d’une, part et trenchans;	The form of the spiny spatumile, which is made into a fistula, is very sharp and pointed on one side.
et d’autre part non, por ceu c’on ne cope mie ceu c’on ne doit mie copeir, si com tu vois ci:	On the other side it is not sharp, so that it should not be bandaged as it should not be, as you see here.
des emorroydes	of hemorrhoids
Emorrydes sont selonc ij. manieres: ou elles sont dedens le fondement, ausi com grain de resin, et s’en i a petites et grans, et en cort adés sanc,	Hemorrhoids are of two types: they can be inside the anus, like grains of resin, and there are small and large ones, and they sometimes leak blood.
et s’en i a une ou plusors, et sont defuer le fondement et au chief dou fondement; mais celles qui sont defuer si ont poc de moistor,	And some protrude from the anus and from the top of the anus; but those that protrude have little moisture.
et encort adés ou un poc d’aigue citrine ou un poc de sanc, et ont la color dou cors;	And they sometimes leak a little water or a little blood, and have the color of the body;
et li cure de ces qui les ont dedens le fondement, si est que tu comandes au malaide qu’il s’espreigne por aleir en chambres, tant que li fondemens li isse fuer, et c’aperent li filz;	And the treatment for those who have them inside the anus is that you instruct the patient to straining to go to the toilet until the hemorrhoids protrude and are visible;
si te haste, et le pent as tenailles, ou tu le tien a ton ungle, puis le cope en ses racines;	if you hurry, and you can grab it with tweezers, or hold it with your fingernail, then pull it out by the roots;
et se li uncine ne les pueent tenir por ses moistors, si les prent a .i. drapeil, ou a couton, ou d’une piece de chamelot;	and if they cannot be held with tweezers due to moisture, then grab them with a piece of cloth, or cotton, or a piece of camel hair;
et les estrai a tes dois, puis les cope, et poudre desus aucunes chaudes poudres que soient en leu de cautere;	and pull it out with your fingers, then crush it, and powder some hot powder on top of it that acts as a cautery;
ou tu les cauterize si com il est dit ou chapistre de cautere, puis les cure d’autres cures tant qu’il soit sanez;	or you can cauterize them as described in the chapter on cauterization, then treat it with other treatments until it is healed;
et se li fondemens ne puet issir, si clisterize le malaide de clistere mordant et aspre por laver ceu qui est ou fondement, si qu’il puist issir apertement;	and if the foundations cannot emerge, then cleanse the patient with a strong and harsh enema to wash away what is in the foundations, so that they can emerge openly.
cant li malaides se preint, et se li fil sont fuer dou fondement, si est li cure legiere;	When the patients defecate, and if the thread is still outside the anus, then the treatment is easy.
et est que tu les preignes a ton ungle ou as tenailles, et les cope, puis les cure si com nos avons dit, tant qu’il soit sanez, et qu’il redoute l’incision par fer.	and you can grab them with your fingernail or tweezers, and cut them, then treat them as we have said, until they are healed and the incision is closed by iron.
Si covient que tu amenistre la costure selonc ceste maniere: pren .i. fil tort, et le boute en une aguille, et puis trai le fil au desus et fai percier l’aguille d’autre part, et torne les .ij. chiez dou fil desoz l’aguille,	If you need to perform surgery in this way: take a twisted thread, and thread it through a needle, then bring the two ends of the thread under the needle from the other side,
et si soit dou large; et estraint le fil forment, puis noe le fil, et estrai l’aguille, et fai ensi de toz les autres, et en laisse .i. por corre la superfluiteit dou sanc;	and if it is too large; and tighten the thread firmly, then tie the thread, and pull out the needle, and do likewise with all the others, and leave one to drain the excess blood;
puis met sus le fondement .i. drapeil moilliet en oile roset ou en cerote, et met sus le fondement, et comande au malaide k’il repose;	then place over the wound a damp cloth moistened with rose oil or cerate, and apply pressure on the wound, and instruct the patient to rest;
et puis le laisse tant qu’il chiecent, et quant il seront cheut, si les cure d’oignement et d’autre cure, tant qu’il soit sanez.	and then let it heal naturally, and once it has healed, treat it with ointments and other remedies until it is completely healed.
dou sechement dou fiens ou fondement	from dryness of the vagina or anus
Maintes fois avient sechement de fiens en l’intestine, et par constrignement de nature, et quant li maladie est vielle et medicine n’i vaut.	Many times there is dryness of the bowels in the intestines, and due to the constraints of nature, and when the illness is old and medicine does not help.
Si covient que tu reses a la point d’un spatumile ou a ton ungle l’escorce desus, qui ne le laisse a moistir;	So you should cut at the tip of a spatula or your nail into the skin on top, which allows moisture to enter.
puis le cure tant qu’il soit sodez si com il covient;	Then dry it until it is stiff as it should be.
et s’il ne puet soder, si rencomence la rasure plus fort que devant, tant qu’il saine mout, et soit escorchiez;	And if it cannot stiffen, then restart the scraping more aggressively than before, until it heals and is scalded.
puis le cure tant qu’il soit sanez.	then treat until healed.
dou fremit	where it trembles
Formice est une petite apparance fautree antor le cors, et va mout em parfont;	Ant is a small appearance wrought under the body, and goes very deep;
et aucune fois la trueve li frois, et le sent on ausi comme mort de fremit, et vient en tout le cors, et plus as mains que autre part.	and sometimes the ant stings, and it feels like death from trembling, and it comes over the whole body, more in the hands than anywhere else.
Et li cure si est que tu pren une cainne d’une penne d’oie, ou une penne de vultul fort, et met celle caine sus le fremit, tant que li cercles porpreigne le fremit tot entor;	And the treatment is that you take a cane of an goose feather, or a strong vulture's feather, and place this cane on the shiver, so that the purple circle the shiver all around.
puis torne ta main a tout la cainne tant que tu copes tout entor le fremit, et le met em parfont, et esraiche le fremit de ses racines.	Then turn your hand to all the cane, so as to stroke all around the shiver, and press it in deeply, and squeeze the shiver from its roots.
Et se tu vues, si fai ceu d’une caine d’arain ou de fer selonc ceste forme, et soit subtilz desoz et traians desus:	And if you see, make it with a cane of bronze or iron according to this form, and let it be thin underneath and drawn out on top.
ne mie perciet, por mues tenir au doi, et mues presser Et se tu vues, si cauterize lou fremit, si com il est devant ou chapistre de cautere.	Do not pierce it, so that it can be held in the hand, and press and squeeze it. And if you see, cauterize the shiver, as it is before in the chapter on cautery.
de la forme dou clistere	of the shape of the enema
Aucune fois fait on clistere d’argent ou d’archaut, ou d’arain fondut ou mailliet; et aucune fois fait on de ces estrumens petis et grans, selonc ces a cui il sont amenistrez.	Sometimes an enema is made of silver or brass, or of molten copper or sheet metal; and sometimes they are made small or large, according to those to whom they are administered.
Cil donques c’on amenistre en la cure des enfans et qui sont foible et dolorous, sont petis.	Those that are administered to children, the weak and sick, should be small.
Li forme dou clistere petit et grant si est desus large, ou li ventres est liiez selonc ceste maniere:	The shape of the enema, whether it is small or large, depends on the width of the rectum, according to this method:
et i ait une desevrance ou li ventres soit liiez, si com tu vois, et li chiez soit dedens perciez; et ait a l’un des costez .ij. pertus, et en l’autre .i.;	and there is an opening where the abdomen is tied, as you see, and the intestines are pierced inside; and it has two holes on one side, and one on the other;
et soit li ventres ou om met les medicines d’une vessie de beste ou de parchemin, et soit perciez tout entor de menus pertus,	and the abdomen where one puts medicines in a beast's bladder or parchment, and it is pierced all around with small holes;
et ait entre chescun pertus .i. doit d’espaice, puis boute en ces pertus .i. fil fort de fil crut tort en .x. ou enqui entor, et assemble le ventre si com est une chievre;	and between each hole there is a distance of one digit, then insert into these holes one strong thread of twisted flax, and tie the abdomen like a goat;
et quant li medicine est dedens, si la lie a l’estrument devant d’un fil fort, puis clisterize; et c’est li forme dou cercle:	and when the medicine is inside, tie it to the instrument with a strong thread, then enema; and this is the form of the circle:
Et soit li medicine ne trop chaude ne trop froide, et oint le chief dou clistere d’oile ou d’aubun d’uef, ou de semblant chose, puis le boute ens legierement;	And let the medicine not be too hot or too cold, and anoint the head of the syringe with oil or egg white, or a similar thing, then insert it gently;
puis l’espreigne li ministres a ses .ij. mains ensamble, tant qu’il soit toz vuis, puis estrai lou clistere, et lieve li malaides ses jambes a la paroit,	Then the minister squeezes it with both hands together until it is empty, then withdraw the syringe and let the patient hold his legs against his body,
et se li medicine vuet issir, si la teigne tant com il puet; et s’il dort une nuit atot, si est plus grans aide.	and if the medicine wants to come out, he should press it as much as he can; and if he sleeps for a night afterward, it is even more helpful.
Et se tu le clisterizes em maladie de decorrement de ventre, et li medicine se haste d’issir, si le rencomence tant qu’il soit sanez.	And if you use the syringe for the sickness of a flowing stomach, and the medicine rushes out, he should repeat it until he is cured.
Et se li emorroide sont ou fondement, ou aposteme, si soit li clistere ausi subtilz com por .i. enfant;	And if the hemorrhoids are in the anus, or an abscess, then let the enema be as thin as for a child.
et c’est li forme dou clistere subtil sus coi li cuir soit estraint:	and this is the form of the thin enema that makes the skin tight:
des plaies	of wounds
Nos avons jai dit en la division la cure des plaies; or vos dirons les cures de mains et de medicine, selonc l’acomplissement.	We have already discussed in the division the cure of wounds; now we will discuss manual and medicinal cures according to their completion.
Je dis que les plaies sont diverses selonc ceu qu’elles sont faites, et selonc les leus ou les plaies sont faites, et de coi elles sont faites.	I say that wounds are diverse according to how they are made, and according to the place where the wounds are made, and what makes them.
Les choses par coi plaies sont faites sont par gitement de piere, et taille d’espee et de couteil, ou de lance ou de fust ou de siette, ou de semblans choses;	The objects that cause wounds are stones thrown with force, and sword and knife cuts, or lance, staff, arrow, or similar objects.
ou que sont faites selonc les leus dou cors, si com plaie que chiet sus le col, ou sus le chief, ou le peis, ou le ventre, ou le foie, et semblans membres;	Or wounds are made according to the places in the body, such as a wound on the neck, head, foot, belly, liver, and similar organs.
et je vos dirai la cure de chescune plaie, et encomencerai as plaies dou chief simples, car li remenbrance venra en son chapistre.	And I will tell you how to treat each wound, and I will begin with simple head wounds, for the discussion will come back around in this chapter.
Je dis que quant simple plaie vient ou chief, et li os n’est brisiez, si pren garde se c’est de gitement de piere ou de semblans choses, et li cuir est toutevoie rompus et est li plaie grans,	I say that when a simple wound comes to the head, and the bone is not broken, one must take care if it is from a stone or similar object, and the skin is still intact but the wound is large,
et tu doutes levement d’aposteme chaut: si le fai tantost sainier de la cephalique meismement s’il vient poc de sanc de la plaie, et soit li sainie au contraire de la partie navree;	and you doubt there is a hot abscess; then have it bled from the cephalic vein immediately if it is bleeding from the wound, and let the bleeding be in the opposite direction to the damaged part;
et eschuisse li malaides repletion de vin et de viandes grosses.	and let the patient avoid rich foods and wine.
Et s’il ne vuet sainier, si soit amenuisie sa viande, et ne boive point de vin, ne ne menjuce point de char;	And if he does not want to be bled, then let his food be diminished, and let him drink no wine, nor eat any meat;
et met sor la plaie, se apostemes chaus i vient, coton moilliet en oile roset soulement, ou en vin stiptice;	and place it on the wound, if a hot abscess develops, use cotton soaked only in rose oil or in astringent wine;
et s’il n’i a aposteme chaut, si met sus la plaie, s’elle est fresche a tout son sanc, et elle n’est muee par l’air, poudre, que je dirai un poc ci aprés;	and if there is no hot abscess, then place on the wound, if it is fresh and bleeding and not moved by air, the powder that I will describe in a little while;
et se li ars l’ait muee, si met sus aucuns oignemens, tant qu’il soit sanez.	and if it has been moved by the air, then place some ointments on it until it is healed.
Et se li plaie est grans si com de tailleure d’espee et de semblans, et les levres ne se pueent assembler par tentes, si les assemble par cousture, si com je dirai as plaies dou ventre, de la costure.	And if the wound is large, like that of a sword, and the lips cannot be brought together by sutures, then bring them together by stitches, as I will describe for wounds in the abdomen, in the rib cage.
Se li plaie est descoverte de l’os, et pent, et ne tient mais que a un poc, si le cope; puis cure la plaie de medicine, et restoure char dure en leu de cuir,	If the wound is exposed to the bone, and open, and only attached by a little bit, then cut it; then cure the wound with medicine, and restore hard flesh in place of skin,
et comande au malaide a mengier grosses viandes, si com testes et froment cuit, ausi com poulz, et semblans choses.	and instruct the patient to eat coarse meats, such as testicles and cooked wheat, as well as poultry, and similar things.
Et se tu trueves ou cuir porriture, et il n’aert a l’os, si cope lou porrit tot, et giete fuer, puis le cure;	And if you find pus in the skin, and it is not near the bone, then cut out the pus completely, and pour it out, then cure it;
et se il ait artere en la plaie ou voine, dont sans cort, et il ne puet estainchier par medicines, si quier l’artere, et se tu la trueves desloie, si la lie d’un fil;	and if there is an artery in the wound or vein, which bleeds profusely and cannot be staunched with medicine, then tie it off with a thread;
et se ceu ne profite mie, si la cauterize.	and if that does not help, cauterize it.
Et se ces plaies sont petites et simples, si est li cure legiere: et est que tu mettes ens ceste poudre qui soude ainsois que li ars l’ait muee.	And if these wounds are small and simple, the treatment is easy: put this powder on so that it will not move until the wound has healed.
Et li maniere de la poudre si est: pren encens une partie; sanc de dragon .ij. parties; chalz vive .iij. parties, et le poudre subtilment,	And the way to make the powder is this: take incense one part, dragon's blood two parts, quicklime three parts, and powdered very finely.
et emple la plaie, et l’estraint forment, tant qu’elle s’aerse bien et se joigne a tout son sanc;	and apply it to the wound, and hold it firmly in place until it heals completely and joins together with the blood.
et puis la lie bien, et la laisse sens desliier, s’elle n’enfle; car on n’oste la madicine tant qu’ele soit sanee.	bind it tightly and leave it loose if it does not swell; for the medicine is not removed until it is healed.
Et aucune fois fait on ceu de chalz soulement, quant on n’ait l’encens ne lou sanc de dragon, mais que li ars n’ait muee la plaie.	And sometimes cautery is done with a hot iron only, when one does not have incense or dragon's blood; but the wound must be moved by the cautery.
Et se li ars ait mueit la plaie, meismement en esteit, si n’i met om mie ceste poudre;	And if the cautery has moved the wound, apply this powder directly to it;
mais met sus aucuns oignemens digestis, ou poulz de farine d’orge faites d’aigue et de miel, tant qu’ele giete bowe;	but place over it some soothing ointments, or a poultice of barley flour made with water and honey, until it becomes soft;
puis le cure d’autres cures tant qu’il soit sanez.	then treat other wounds until they are healed.
Et se li brisure d’os vient avec la plaie, et elle est petite, si l’estrai as pinceures subtilz;	And if the fracture of the bone comes with the wound, and it is small, I will pull it out with fine pincers;
et je vos dirai ci aprés les brisures dou chief.	and I will tell you about fractures of the head later.
de la plaie dou col	of a wound on the neck
Se plaie vient ou col et elle est simple, si n’a point de difference entre li et celi dou chief, mais se li ners dou col ou li artere est copee.	If the wound is in the neck and it is simple, there is no difference between it and that of the head, but if the nerve of the neck or artery is cut.
Se c’est li ners, si n’i a autre engien que laissier la cure, et n’i mettre nulle chose restraignant, car il nuit as ners et les fait retraire;	If it is the nerve, there is nothing else to do but let it be, and not put anything constricting on it, because it harms the nerves and makes them withdraw.Se c’est li artere, si convient la curer et faire sangler, car elle ne doit point rester ou leu qu’elle est.
et ne mettre sus la plaie rien froit, car li substance des ners est froide, et li continuation d’aus si est avec le cerveil, qui est li plus haus membres;	And nothing cold should be placed on the wound, because the substance of the nerves is cold, and their continuation is with the brain, which is the highest member.Et il convient que l’on fasse le sangler et la cure, car elle ne doit point demorer ou leu qu’elle est, si adone li maux est grant;
mais soit li medicine souez, si com chalz lavee en aigue douce, et mellee avec oile roset, et cucie lavee ausi en aigue douce,	But let the medicine be under him, as hot water washed in cold water, and mixed with rose oil, and cooked washed also in cold water,and if he has a headache or fever or pain anywhere, let him be bled, so that he may be relieved of his illness.Et s’il a male de chief ou fievre ou douleur en quelque lieu, fasse sangler pour qu’il soit delivrez de sa maladie;
et autres pieres de mine selonc ceste maniere, et oignemens moistes.	and other moist stones according to this method, and moist ointments.
Et se li plaie est grans, si la cout et lie de bendes, puis la cure tant qu’il soit sanez.	And if the wound is large, cut it and bind it with bandages, then treat it until it is healed.
Et se les plaies sont parfondes et ele est chevee et pleinne de bowe, si la perce ou plus bas leu;	And if the wounds are deep, and she is pregnant and full of bowels, then pierce her or lower;
et se li artere est copee, et decorremens de sanc en vient, si la desoivre, et la loie, et la cauterize se mestier est;	and if the artery is cut, and bleeding ensues, then ligate it, and stop it, and cauterize it if necessary;
et se li espinee de la gorge est copee, ou li keurs, et li conduiz est gardez, par coi la viande va,	and if the spine of the throat is cut, or the neck, and the windpipe is kept intact, through which the food goes,
si cout le keur sus la cainne de la gorge, et ne touchier la gorge mais la remet selonc sa figure naturel;	if he cuts the neck above the Adam's apple, and doesn't touch the throat but puts it back into its natural shape,
et puis l’estrain avenanment, et le laisse aucuns jors, puis le cure d’oignemens desechans tant qu’il soit sanez;	and then he stretches it gently and leaves it for several days, then he treats it with cleansing ointments until it is healed;
et se li plaie a fait empression en l’os, si la quier;	and if the wound has made an impression on the bone, then it will;
et s’il i a pieces d’os, si les trai fuers toz se tu pues, et ces que tu ne pues avoir, si laisse tant que li plaie porrisse,	and if there are pieces of bone, pull them out as much as you can, and those that you cannot reach, leave them until the wound can heal.
et soit desevree et aligie li issue;	and then clean and bind up the dislocation.
et se li plaie est fresche, si poudre sus la poudre que j’ai dit.	and if the wound is fresh, apply the powder I have described.
Et s’il a en la plaie os et il i a fistule, si la cure ensi com j’ai dit en son chapistre.	And if there is bone in the wound and there is a fistula, treat it as I have described in its chapter.
de la plaie de lance ou de coutel	of the wound from a spear or knife
Se c’est cop de lance ou de coutel, et li plaie est parfonde, si regarde se de la plaie saut ventositez cant li malaides alainne: saiches adonques que li plaie est mortelz;	If it is a spear or knife wound, and the wound is deep, then examine if from the wound issues blood and pus: know therefore that the wound is deadly;
et s’elle n’est parfonde, et elle est fresche a tout son sanc, si n’i mettre mie a la premiere houre la poudre, ne ne la liier mie por le sanc que ne demorse em parfont,	and if it is not deep and the wound is fresh and bleeding with its own blood, then do not apply powder to it at first or ligature it for fear of the blood clotting deeply;
et reviegne au cuer, et ocie lou malaide;	and let the patient rest and recover;
mais i met oignement atractif, et le lie .ij. fois le jor;	but apply an attractive ointment, and bind it .ii. times a day;
et se tu n’as oignement, si met en la plaie viel coton por succier fuers la moistor,	and if you do not have ointment, put old cotton in the wound to draw out moisture,
et fai dormir le malaide sus la plaie .iij. jors, ou .iiij., ou plusors;	and let the patient sleep on the wound for .iii. days, or .iv., or more;
si n’i venra mie spasme, ne tremor male de cuer n’es traingnemens d’alainne;	if there is no spasms, nor tremors, nor pains in the heart, nor twitches of the limbs;
et quant tu vois les bones dispositions, si saiches que li plaie est sauve.	and when you see the bones back in alignment, then you know the wound is healed.
Cure la donques de tentes et d’autres cures, tant qu’il soit sanez;	Treat it with poultices and other remedies until it is healed;
et s’elle ne puet saner, et oevre, adés saiches que il i a fistule; si la cure si com on doit.	and if it cannot heal, and there is still discharge, then you know that there is a fistula; treat it as needed.
Et se li plaie est d’incision d’espee ou de coutel, et elle est simple, ou pis ou au dos, si la cure de ceu qui est devant;	And if the wound is from a sword or knife, and it is simple, or on the top or bottom, treat it as follows:
s’elle est grans, de cousture; et s’elle est petite, de poudre, et s’elle est empressee en l’os, et en a copeit pieces, si quier la plaie, et les trai fuers s’il sont desevrez;	if it is large, with sewing; and if it is small, with powder, and if it is pressed into the bone, and has pieces broken off, then the wound, and the arrows, if they are stuck in, must be pulled out.
et s’il ne sont desevrez, si laisse porrir la plaie, si aligera li estractions;	and if they are not stuck in, let the wound fester, so that it will heal.
et des autres plaies as autres membres est li jugemens si com nos avons dit.	and for other wounds on other body parts, the judgement is as we have said.
dou derrompement dou ventre	rupture of the belly
Li derompemens dou ventre est grans et moiens et petis;	There are great, medium, and small ruptures of the belly;
de la grant plaie saut aucune fois li intestine, ou li ners des intestines, par coi li intromission d’aus;	from the large wound sometimes the intestines, or the nerves of the intestines, emerge, through which the entrance of air occurs;
et li costure est plus malaisie, et aucune fois vaut pis li petite plaie que li grans,	and the cure is more difficult, and sometimes the small wound is worse than the large one,
por ceu c’on remet plus a poinnes les intestines en, s’on ne les i remet de chaut en chaut;	because one returns the intestines to their place with pins, if one does not return them gradually from hot to cold;
por ce que li intestine enflent tantost qu’il sentent le froit, si rentrent plus a poinnes,	for the intestines, when they feel cold, quickly return inside.
et por ceu vaut mues li moieinne plaie, por ceu c’on ramoine mues l’intestine a son leu que as autres .ij.	and therefore, it is necessary to massage the soft wound, and therefore we must massage the intestines into their place along with the others [2.10]
Et saiches que li routure dou ventre est selonc .iiij. manieres:	And know that hernia of the abdomen occurs in four ways:
les .ij. costures communes avienent en la costure dou ventre,	the two common hernias occur in the abdominal wall,
et li costure des autres plaies dou cors et .ij. autres costures propres sont communes as autres plaies;	and the stitching of other wounds on the body, and another two stitches specific to the wound are common to other wounds;
et toutevoie elles sont plus propres avec la costure dou ventre, et je dirai une chescune et declairerai.	yet they are more appropriate with the stitching of the abdomen, and I will describe each one and clarify.
Je di que quant li plaie est petite, et aucune chose de l’intestine ist fuer,	I say that when the wound is small, and some intestines protrude,
et griés chose est dou remettre, ceu est par l’une des .ij. manieres:	and the injury is slight, it can be treated by one of two methods:The following text is a medieval medical treatise written in Old French, around the 12th-13th centuries.
ou por la petitece de la plaie, si com nos avons dit,	or through the smallness of the wound, as we have said,
ou por ce que li intestine est enflez por le froit.	or because the intestines are swollen from the cold.
Et quant il est frois, eschaufez lou en teil maniere:	And when it is cold, heat it in this manner:
moillie une esponge ou .i. mol drapeil en aigue tede soulement,	wet a sponge or soft cloth with only lukewarm water,
ou tu cuis en aigue squinant et cipre et spique,	or you cook in water squint and cypress and spike,
et arose l’intestine tant que li enfleure soit ostee;	and boil the intestines until they are swollen;
et aucune fois fait ce vins restraingnans, et est muedre que awe soule por desenfler.	and sometimes makes this restraining wine, and it is milked that it may soothe.
Et quant tu vois l’enfleure departir, si amoiste l’intestine d’aigue ou altee et malves soient cuites,	And when you see the swelling depart, then mix the intestines with water or old wine and let them cook,
car par ceu est aligie li entree a poc de chose;	for through this, the entrance is restricted to a small amount;
et s’il n’i puet entrer, si fent un poc la plaie a l’estrument de coi on cope les emorroydes;	and if it cannot enter, then they make an incision in the instrument with which they cut hemorrhoids;
et li premiere cure est muedre que li taille,	and the first cure is bloodletting rather than cutting,
que nus n’i doit taillier sens grant necessiteit n’i ait;	and one should not cut without great necessity;
et c’est li estrumens por le fendre:	and this is the instrument to split it with:
si trenche dedens en la corbeure et defuer non, et vez ci la forme:	if cut inside the curve and not out, and observe the form here:
Et quant li plaie est enlargie, et li intestine saut fuer,	And when the wound is enlarged and the intestines jump out,
si le remet arer selonc la forme naturel en son leu propre,	if one puts it back according to its natural form in its proper place,
se tu en as pooir, car ce vaut mues.	if you can, for this is best.
Quant li plaie est large, et elle est en la partie desoz lou ventre,	When the wound is large and it is in the lower part of the belly,
si covient que tu faices gesir lou malaide sus son dos,	you should have the patient lie on his back,
et met ses jambes plus haut que son chief;	and his legs higher than his head;
et s’elle est en la partie desoz le ventre,	and if it is in the lower part of the belly,
si met le chief et le pis plus haut que les parties desoz,	place the head and feet higher than the parts below,
et ausi se li routure dou ventre est en l’une des .ij. parties	and also if the ruture of the belly is in one of the .ij. parts
si met t’entente en ceu que li partie navree soit plus haute que li autre;	if you place your understanding so that the wounded part is higher than the other;
et ensi covient amenistrer ceu que je dis en plaies grans et moienes.	and thus one must treat those who are large and medium sized wounds.
Es plaies petites met ceu que t’est apparilliet,	For small wounds, use what you have available,
puis aies entre tes mains .i. ministre pitous ki teigne toute la routure a sa main,	then have at hand a minister of pity who will put his entire hand on the wound,
et assemble les levres;	and bring together the lips;
et c’est la maniere commune de costures,	and this is the common method of sewing.
et est que tu preignes une aguille ou plusors, selonc la quantiteit de la largesce de la plaie,	take a needle or several, depending on the width of the wound,
puis laisse des le chief de la plaie .i. doi d’espaice, et i fiche une aguille ou il ait .i. boin fil fort;	then leave a distance of one finger from the edge of the wound and insert a needle with a strong thread through it;
et perce les .ij. chiés dou cuir avec les .ij. chiés dou siphac,	and pierce the two edges of the skin with the two edges of the wound,
qui est desoz le cuir dedens, tant que tu la faices percier de celle partie,	which is under the skin inside, until you make it pierce from that part,
et assemble les .ij. chief dou siphac les .iiij. ensamble;	and bring together the two heads of the bone into alignment with the four ends;
puis l’estrain d’un fil double entor l’aguille de .ij. pars,	then draw it together with a double thread around an awl in two places,
puis assemble les .ij. chiés de la plaie avenanment,	and then bring together the two heads of the wound smoothly,
et puis laisse .i. doi d’espaice, et i fiche une autre aguille;	and then leave. I put a distance of two fingers, and I stick another needle;
puis la lie dou fil si com tu as fait la premiere aguille,	then tie the thread as you did with the first needle,
et ne cesser de ceu faire selonc ceu que tu as mestier des aguilles,	and do not stop doing this according to what you need of needles,
tant que toute li plaie soit restrainte;	until all the wound is restrained;
et soient les aguilles moienes, entre subtilz et grosses,	and let the needles be medium-sized, between thin and thick,
car les aguilles subtilz copent toute la char, et les trop grosses si ne pueent mie bien entrer:	because thin needles pierce all the flesh, and very thick ones cannot enter well.
por ceu covient qu’elles soient moienes;	therefore they should be medium-sized;
et ne covient mie bouter les aguilles trop au defuer de la char et dou cuir,	and one must not push the needles too deep into the flesh and through the skin,
k’elles ne copent et oevrent la plaie devant la soudure;	that they do not cut and open the wound before the scabs form;
et puis cope les chiés des aguilles, qu’elles ne blecent lou malaide au dormir,	and then cut the head of the needles so that they do not pricke the patient when he sleeps,
et i met tentes ou drapelz au chiés des aguilles por mues tenir,	and put tents or bandages on the heads of the needles to keep them in place,
et les laisse tant que li plaie soit soudee;	and leave them until the wound is closed.
et ceste maniere de costure as aguilles est plus covenauble en petites plaies,	and this method of sewing with needles is most suitable for small wounds,
car il i soffist une aguille ou .ij.	because one or two needles are enough.
Li seconde costure si est commune,	The second stitch is common,
et est que tu assemble les .ij. chiés dou cuir et les .ij. chiés dou syfac ensamble a une aguille ou il ait .i. fort fil moien;	and is where you join the two edges of the skin and the two edges of the wound together with one needle and a strong, thin thread;
et quant tu avras perciez ces chiez toz .iiij. ensamble,	and when you have pierced all four of these joints together,
si ramoinne l’aguille a la partie ou tu as encomenciet, en la maniere c’on cout les dras;	then reset the needle at the part where you began, in the way they sew up clothes;
et met d’espaice entre chescune costure la grossece d’un menor doi;	and put a distance between each stitch equal to the thickness of a thumb nail;
ceste costure sevent li home,	this stitching is for a man,
et je cousi une plaie c’uns hons avoit ou ventre,	and I sewed up a wound that a man had on his belly,
qui estoit navrez d’un coutel,	which had been made by a knife,
et estoit li plaie plus d’une palme de grant,	and the wound was more than a palm in length,
et issoit des intestines bien .ij. palmes de grant,	and the intestines protruded out more than two palms,
et estoit li plaie enmi le ventre.	and the wound was near the navel.
Je li ramenai l’intestine puis k’il ot esteit .xxiiij. houres fuer,	I returned his intestines to their proper place after they had been outside his body for twenty-four hours.
et fut li plaie soudee jusc’a .xv. jors, et le curai, et fut sanez.	And the wound was sewn up until the fifteenth day, and I treated it, and it healed.
Et li mire l’avoient jugiet qu’il morroit, et ce fut miracle;	And they had judged that he would die, and this was a miracle;
et ne le curai mie d’oignement, car je estoie en .i. leu ou on n’en trovoit point, ne nule medicines;	and I did not treat it with ointment, because I was in a place where there were no ointments or medicines to be found;
et metoie sens plus sus la plaie coton viel .ij. fois le jor, et le lavoie d’aigue de miel tant qu’il fut sanez.	and I applied old cotton twice a day to the wound and washed it with honey water until it healed.
Or vos dirai les .ij. propres manieres de cousture:	Now I will tell you about two proper methods of suturing:
pren l’aguille, et la boute des la partie defuers jusc’a celi dedens;	take the needle and pierce it through from one side to the other;
quant elle a perciet le keur de droit en droit, si lai le chief dou siphac ou cousteit ou tu as bouteit l’aguille,	when it has pierced through the heart from right to right, then place the needle in the back of the throat.
et la fai percier d’autre part des la partie dedens jusc’a celi defuer;	and pierce it through from the other side of that part all the way to the chest;
et li entendemens de ceste costure si est que tu cous ausi com li peletier font les pelz,	and the meaning of this sewing is that you sew as the leather-workers do with skins,
et que tu laisses une fois le syfac d’une part, et le reprent d’autre, tant que li costure soit toute acomplie.	and let one side of the throat hang loose while you tighten the other, until the sewing is complete.
Li seconde maniere de costure, que Galiens dist proprement,	The second method of stitching, which Galen describes properly,
si est si com aucun font, qui assemblent les .ij. parties ensamble naturelment,	is if it is like two pieces of wood that are joined together naturally,
et apploient l’un des chief dou syfac a l’autre chief, en teil maniere:	and they apply the end of one piece to the other, in such a way:
fiche une aguille ou chief dou mirach prochiene, et fai percier celui leu soulement,	stick an awl or needle into the nearest part, and only pierce that area,
et laisse les .ij. chiés dou syfac;	let the two shoulders of the syringe
puis torne l’aguille, et la fai percier des la partie defuers jusc’a celi dedens,	then turn the needle and pierce it from the outside part just to the inside,
as .ij. chiés dou syfac;	so as to let the two shoulders of the syringe.
puis fai percier l’un et l’autre des la partie defuers jusc’a celi dedens, en .ij. autres chiés dou mirach que sont on l’autre costeit;	then pierce one and the other from the outside part just to the inside, in two other shoulders of the mirach that are on the other side;
et c’est li muedre maniere de costure et li plus commune.	and this is the best way to sew and the most common.
Galiens si dist ceste parolle, et aucun le tesmoignent,	Galen says these words, and some testify to it,
c’on doit coudre le ventre a .ij. aguilles, ou il ait fil en chescune;	that one should sew the belly with two needles, with thread in each;
et doit on bouter l’une aguille d’une part, et l’autre d’autre, en la maniere de ces qui cousent corroies;	and one needle from one side and the other from the other, in the manner of those who sew shoes;
et saiches que quant li routure est enmi lou ventre,	and you know that when the hernia is in the abdomen,
si est li cousture plus griez que des autres leus dou ventre.	the incision is deeper than other places in the belly.
Li jugemens de la plaie si est telz com li jugemens des autres plaies:	The judgment of the wound is such as the judgment of other wounds:
et est que quant tu trueves la plaie fresche a tout son sanc, ainsois que li ars l’ait muee,	and it is that when you find the fresh wound all its blood, as long as the flesh has not moved,
si remet arer l’intestine, et lou cout; puis met sus la poudre enjanrant char,	if one wants to put back the intestine, and sew it up; then put on the powder of black gall.
et se li ars l’ait muee, si met sus aucun oignement que soit present, tant que li plaie bowe;	and if there is any movement in the wound, put on some ointment that is available until it heals.
et chicent li fil, et soient soudez li sifac, et li mirach;	and they sew up the thread, and seal the sutures, and the mastic;
puis cure la plaie si com les autres, tant qu’il soit sanez;	then heal the wound as with the others, until it is healed;
et se tu n’as medicines, si met sus, tantost qu’ele comance a giter bowe, coton viel,	and if you have no medicine, then put on, as soon as it begins to drip, old cotton,
et le remue .ij. fois le jor tant k’il soit sanez.	and move it twice a day until it heals.
Car tu n’as mestier d’autre medicine en plusors dispositions cant les plaies sont simples;	For you do not need any other medicine for various wounds when they are simple;
et se tu doutes que li plaie ne faice communiteit as membres principelz,	and if you doubt that the wound is causing infection in the principal members,
si covient ke tu moilles lainne legiere en oile de tempree chalor, ou en oile roset,	then you must moisten a light woolen cloth with tempered oil or rose oil.
et la met entor les angres, et desoz les asselles;	and place it around the wounds and under the armpits.
et s’il sent dolor ou porriture en bouelz, et maintes fois avient,	and if he feels pain or swelling in the groin, which often occurs,
si les clisterize de vin noir tede, et meismement se li porriture vient jusc’a l’intestine;	you must place it around the wounds and under the body and head; you should also use enemas of warm red wine, especially if the swelling extends to the intestines.
et le perce dedens, et saiches que quant c’est li gros intestines, si est plus legier a saner que li petis.	and it pierces inside, and know that when it is the large intestine, it is easier to heal than the small one.
Li intestine qui est apelez «jeun» ne puet saner quant il est navrez,	The intestine which is called "young" cannot heal when it is raw,
et c’est por la planteit des voinnes que i sont, et por la subtiliteit de tout le cors, et l’aprochement de sa nature des ners.	and it's because of the thinness of the veins that they are, and because of the subtlety of the whole body, and the proximity to its nature of the nerves.
Et si li zirbe saut de la plaie, si le remet arrier ausi com l’intestine, tandis qu’il est fres;	And if the zarbe jumps out of the wound, he puts it back as well as the intestine, while it is fresh;
et s’il est vielz et devenus vers ou noir, si covient que tu lies le leu qui est noir, que decorremens de sanc n’i viegne,	and if it is old and turned black or blue, then you should tie off the area that is black so that no more blood flows to it,
car il i a voinnes et arteres;	because there are veins and arteries in it;
puis cope ceu qui est entre le liien,	then cut what is between the ligature,
et met les .ij. chiés pendans des la partie desoz la plaie jusque defuer por aligier l’estraction quant li zirbes chiet, et li plaie bowe.	and put the two pieces hanging from the part below the wound until it is healed to aid in extraction when the scabs fall off, and the wound heals.
de la routure dou boueil	of the road of the boil
Quant li intestine est rons, et li plaie est petite,	When the intestines are ruptured, and the wound is small,
si la puet on restorer en aucuns homes,	one can repair it in some people,
por ceu que je vis que uns hons fut navrez ou ventre d’une lance;	because I saw a man who was pierced in the belly by a spear;
et estoit li plaie au destre de l’estomac,	and the wound was on the right side of the stomach,
et fut envillie et devint fistule, et en issoit li egestion et li ventositez;	and it became a fistula, and discharged pus and gas;
je i mis cure selonc ceu que je poi, et ne cessai de subtilier tant qu’il fut sanez, et li leus soudez.	I treated it with cauterization according to what I could, and did not cease until it was healed and the wounds closed.
Et quant je le vis souder, je doutai que li malaides n’eust mal en son ventre;	And when I saw it healing, I doubted that the patient had pain in his belly;
et il n’i ot point de mal, mais demora en millors dispositions, et menjans et bevans;	and he had no ill effects, but remained in better condition, eating and drinking;
et dirent aucun experimentors que quant il a petite plaie en l’intestine, qu’il doit estre liiez en teil maniere:	some experimentalists say that when there is a small wound in the intestine, it should be bound in such a way:
pren fremis a grans testes, puis assemble les levres de la plaie,	take cow's guts, then bring together the lips of the wound,
et quant li fremis ait overte la bouche, si la met sus les .ij. levres,	and when the gut has opened its mouth, place it on both lips,
si qu’elle estraigne sa bouche sus;	so that he opens his mouth upward;
et puis li cope la teste, et ce se tient si qu’il ne puet desliier,	and then press his head, and it will remain so that he cannot loosen it,
puis met .i. autre fremit aprés en celle maniere que devant, tant que li plaie soit toute porprise;	then put another splint in the same manner as before, until the wound is completely closed;
et cout la plaie.	and bind the wound.
Cil chief si s’aerdent en l’intestine, et ne vient nulle nuisance au malaide,	If they grow in the intestines and cause no harm to the patient,
et se puet on liier l’intestine d’un fil subtil qui est copez de l’intestine d’une beste,	and one can tie the intestine with a thin string cut from the intestine of an animal,
en teil maniere:	in such a way:
pren le chief de cest fil d’intestine que soit mout descharnez,	take the end of this intestine string that is very dry,
et puis lie au chief de cest fil .i. fil de lin subtil tort,	and then tie to the head of this thread a thread of fine twisted flax
puis boute le fil en l’aguille, et en cout l’intestine, et le ramoinne en la routure;	then thread the needle and pierce the gut, and sew it up again;
et ceste maniere de costure de fremis nen est fuers que selonc la voie de fiance et d’esperance;	and this manner of sewing up the intestines is not safe except according to the way of faith and hope;
et se li plaie est grans et large, meismement quant elle est en l’un des grailes intestines, si n’i a engien ne santeit, fuer que subtiliteit.	and if the wound is large and wide, especially when it is in one of the small intestines, there is no healing or health without subtlety.
de fistule ou qu’ele soit	of fistula wherever it may be
Saiches que toute plaie ou aposteme, quant il enveillist, si est apelee universement «fistule»,	You should know that any wound or abscess, when it becomes open and suppurates, is universally called a "fistula."
et meismement quant elle est chevee et rent bowe.	And likewise, when it becomes closed and heal shut.
Et fistule est selonc la verteit nodation fautree dure et blainche, ou on ne sent dolor,	And a fistula is according to the green, knotted, hard and white suppuration, where one feels no pain,
et est ausi chevee com li penne d’un oiseil;	and is also shaped like a bird's feather;
et aucune fois en saut clere bowe, et autre fois espesse;	sometimes they are long and clear, and sometimes thick;
aucune fois poc, et autre fois assez;	sometimes they are small, and sometimes large enough;
et je en ai jai parleit en la division des plaies, que toute plaie que n’est sanee, et il n’i a char,	I have spoken of this in the division of wounds, that any wound which is not healed and there is no scar,
ce n’est fuers que par une des .viiij. causes:	except for one of the eight causes;
c’est a savoir, par la petitece dou sanc ou cors;	that is to say, through a small wound in blood vessels or flesh;
ou por sa malice;	or due to maliciousness;
ou por ceu qu’il i a char dure dedens, et sus les levres, que n’i laisse naistre char;	or because there is a hard lump inside, and on the lips, that does not allow lumps to form;
ou il i a trop de bowe;	or he has too much bowels;
ou li leus est porris, et li matiere est de male qualiteit;	or his skin is porous, and the material of poor quality;
ou li medicine n’est mie bone en la cure;	or the medicine is not good for the treatment;
ou por ceu que li corruption est maniere de pestilence;	or because the putrefaction is of a pestilential nature;
ou por la proprieteit en la region est tardive li digestion, et tarde li santeit, et enflee par nature;	or because of the property of the region, digestion is late, health comes slowly, and it swells by nature;
ou il i a voinnes ou os:	or there are veins or bones:
et j’ai ja mostreit toutes ces causes, et les signes, et les cures de medicines en la division.	and I have already shown all these causes, and the signs, and the cures of medicines in the division.
Or covient que je te faice a savoir la cure de fistule qui est faite par oevre de mains.	Now I will tell you about the treatment for a fistula that is done by hand.
Saiches que fistule avient en tous membres dou cors;	Know that a fistula occurs in all parts of the body;
car il i a fistules que vienent as grans voines, et as arteres, et as ners,	for there are fistulas that come from large veins, and arteries, and nerves,
ou au syfac, ou a l’intestine, ou a la vessie, ou a aucunes des costes,	or in the face, or intestines, or bladder, or some of the sides,
ou a l’espinee dou dos, ou a aucune jointe des mains ou des piez;	or in the spine of the back, or in any joint of the hands or feet;
et si a teil que vient a la proprieteit dou membre principeil, et as semblans leus.	and if it affects the principal organ, and similar places.
Et toutes les fistules que sont de ceste maniere sont de grief sanation, et n’i a fors que labour, et ignorance;	And all the fistulas that are in this way, they are of grief sanation, and there is no remedy but labor and ignorance;
et se il i a aucune fistule que ne veigne mie jusc’a leu que j’ai dit, et tu as fiance de la cure,	and if there is any fistula that does not come to the place that I have said, and you have faith in the cure,
et tu la vues conoistre, si pren une tente d’arain ou de fer, se li fistule est droite, si la quier;	and you want to know it, take an iron or bronze tent, if the fistula is straight, put it on;
et se li fistule est torte, si la cerche d’une subtil tente de plonc,	and if the fistula is crooked, then search for a thin, blunt probe
car li plons se ploie mues entor la tortuositeit;	because the probe bends with the curvature.
et se li fistule a mains pertus et tu ne la pues mie bien cerchier par tentes,	and if the fistula is wide and you cannot probe it well,
si la clisterize par l’un des pertus,	then cleanse it through one of the openings,
car la moistors si cort d’un pertus a autre, et la mundifie;	for moisture quickly travels from one orifice to another and purifies.
puis la quier saigement a ton pooir, que tu conoisses s’il i a os ou nerf, et est chevee em parfont,	then you will know if there is bone or nerve involved, and it is deeply embedded.
et demande bien au malaide de la dolor qu’il sent au presser de ta main, et le leu ou il la sent;	and ask the patient about the pain they feel when you press with your hand, and where they feel it.
et quant tu savras vraiement le leu ou elle est, et s’elle est loing de jointure, ou de nerf, ou d’artere ou de voine,	and when you know for sure the location, whether it is far from a joint, nerve, artery, or vein,
ou en aucuns des leus que je t’ai dit, si la cope selonc ceu que je t’ai dit,	or in any of the ways I have told you, the cup according to what I have said to you,
et oste fuer la fautreure et les chars corrumpues que sont dedens;	and remove the soiled and rotten clothes that are inside;
et puis la cure tant qu’elle soit sanee,	and then clean the wound until it is healed,
et se li fistule est bien parfonde de droit endroit, si covient que tu copes em parfont, tant com tu pues,	and if the fistula is very deep in a straight line, you must cup it deeply as much as you can,
puis i met tentes moillies en medicine ague, et les boute jusc’au chief de la fistule,	then I apply wet bandages on the medicine to the head of the fistula
tant que li medicine corrode la superfluiteit qui est demoree au fons;	until the medicine corrodes the excess which remains at the bottom;
et puis i met oignemens enjanrans sainne char, tant qu’il soit sanez;	and then I apply warming ointments to healthy flesh until it is healed;
et s’il n’est sanez par ceu, si le cauterize si com nos avons dit,	and if it is not healed by this, then cauterize it as we have said,
et se li os est corrompus de la fistule, si le cope.	and if the bone is corrupted by the fistula, cut it away.
Se voinne ou ners ne te greve ou membres principelz, si com nos avons dit;	If a vein or nerve troubles you in your principal limbs, as we have said;
et se li os est descovers, et il i a corruption et noiror, si lou reis tant que li corruption soit toute ostee,	and if the bone is uncovered and there is corruption and blackness, then cut it away until all the corruption is removed,
puis le cure de choses enjanrans char tant qu’il soit sanez;	then cleanse it with lye water until it is clean;
et s’il n’est sanez, et rent bowe si com devant,	and if it is not healthy, return it as before,
saiches que tu n’es mie alez jusc’a font:	know that you have not gone to the well;
si descuevre et quier tant que tu soies au fons,	uncover and desire as much as you are at the bottom,
et oste toute la corruption, puis restore le leu;	and remove all corruption, then restore the place;
et s’il est ensi sanez, c’est bien.	and if it is thus without pain, that is good.
Se ceu non, saiches que la corruption est trop en parfont, que tu n’i pues avenir;	if not, know that the corruption is too deep for you to reach;
si n’i a autre engien que dou lassier a nature;	and if there is no other way except by the knife;
et s’il i a i petit os corrumput, et tu le pues traire as tenailles,	and if there is a small rotten bone that you can pull out with tweezers,
si l’estrai a .i. estrument covenauble a ceu,	if you extract it with a suitable instrument for this purpose,
et s’il i a maint os, si les trai trestoz, ne n’en laissier nes un;	and if there are many bones, pull them all out without leaving any behind;
et se li moistor te fait contraire, et il n’i a error ne paour,	and if the moisture makes it difficult, and there is no error or fear,
si cope et moistor et char, et delivre les os.	pull out the bone from the flesh and moisture.
Et se tu ne les pues oster a une houre, si met sus la plaie chose enjanrant porriture,	And if you cannot remove them in one hour, then place something on the wound to encourage pus.
et laisse tant que li leus soit porris entor les os,	and let it be until the pus runs around the bone,
et adonc si avront plus legierement les os;	and then they will have the bones more easily;
et se c’est uns grans os, si com de jambe ou de cuisse,	and if it is a large bone, such as the leg or thigh,
si reis tant soulement la corruption tant que li noiror soit toute ostee,	if you simply treat the infection until the darkness is completely gone,
puis restoure la plaie;	then restore the wound;
et s’il en i a grant partie dou corrumput, et vient jusc’a mole de l’os;	and if there is a large amount of corruption, and it reaches to the bone;
si le covient soier et coper tout jusc’a la corruption, et puis le cure tant qu’il soit soudez;	if necessary, cut away and cover all the way to the corruption, and then cure it until it is healed;
et je te dirai d’une fistule qui avint .i. home en sa jambe,	I will tell you about a fistula which happened to a man on his leg.
si que tu i preignes exemple et aide en ton ovraige.	so that you can take example and help in your work.
Il fut .i. jovencelz entor .xxx. ans, qui ot une dolor en sa jambe d’une cause que vint dedens le cors,	He was a young man of about 30 years who had pain in his leg from a cause that came from inside the body,
tant que les matieres vinrent a la jambe, et fut enflee d’un gros aposteme, et n’ot point de cause defuer por ovrir;	such that the matter came to the leg, and it was swollen with a large abscess, and had no cause to open;
mais li mire par lor folie ovrerent tant sus que li apostemes ovri,	but they miraculously worked so much that the abscesses opened
et en corroient mout de matieres, et devint fistule, et i vint mout de pertus que tuit gitoient bowe et moistor dou cors;	and much matter flowed out and it became a fistula, and many openings appeared from which pus and moisture flowed from the body;
et maint mire i mirent cure entor .ij. ans, et n’i ot nul saige en l’art de mains,	and many had treatment for two years, and there was no wise man in the art of medicine,
tant que je i fui apelez, et vi sa jambe et les medicines dont on le curoit,	as long as I was called to see him, and saw his leg and the medicines with which he was treated,
et ceu que corroit par les pertus a grant cors;	and what ran through the holes with great force;
et devenoit rouges li cors dou jouvenceil, et avoit color citrine.	and became red on the bodies of young people, and had a yellow color.
Je boutai une tente en l’un de ces pertus, et puis cerchai toz les pertus,	I pitched a tent at one of these openings, and then investigated all the openings,
et trovai que li uns venoit encontre l’autre de toutes les parties de la jambe.	and found that they came together in pairs from all parts of the leg.
Je me hastai donques, et copai en l’un des pertus tant que je descovri une partie de l’os,	I therefore hurried, and struck at one of the openings until I exposed a portion of bone.
et le trovai corrumput et perciet, et venoit li corruption jusc’a l’os dedens;	And found it rotten and pierced, the corruption going right through to the bone within.
je soiai ceu qui m’aparissoit de l’os corrumput, et cuidai qu’il n’i eust autre corruption, fuer que celi que je ostai;	I removed what appeared to be rotten bone, and believed that there was no other corruption except for that which I removed.
et comensai a restourer la plaie de medicines sodans par lonc tens, et ne pot souder;	And began to dress the wound with strong medicines over a long time, but it would not heal.
et puis rencomensai, et descovri l’os si com devant,	and then restart, and expose the bone as before,
et trovai la corruption continuee en l’os, et la soiai, et puis l’ostai, et me penai de souder le leu;	and found the corruption continued in the bone, and I cut it out, and then removed it, and worked to sew up the area;
mais je ne pou tant que je copai entor une palme de l’os, et le traï fuer a tout son mole,	but I could not reach more than a palm's width into the bone, so I left it half-done,
puis le restourai de medicines; et il fut sanez et soudez hastanment,	then I treated it with medicine; and it healed and closed up quickly,
et ne covint plus rencomencier l’ovraige fors por la foibleté dou malaide, qui ne pooit soffrir,	and it is not necessary to repeat the procedure except for the weakness of the patient who cannot endure it,
et por la paour de mort que je avoie de lui.	and out of fear of his death which I had for him.
Car por l’evacuation sanglotoit sovent, mais il fut sanez entierement,	For through the evacuation of blood he often bled, but he was completely healed
et nasquit en leu de l’os une char dure, et fut de bone disposition et n’ot point de nuisement ne de contraire dou tout en tout, ne a l’aleir ne a venir.	and there grew in place of the bone a hard scar, and he was of good disposition and had no harm or contrary effect at all, neither in walking nor coming.
Et se li os est brisiez en aucun leu dou cors, si le covient soier en ceste maniere:	And if the bone is broken anywhere in the body, it must be set in this way:
pren .i. liien, et l’estrain au chief de l’os qui apert,	Take a thread and stretch it tightly to the head of the exposed bone,
et comande aucun k’il l’estende en haut;	and have someone else hold it tightly upward;
et met .i. autre lien de lainne plus gros dou premier liien, et le lie sus la char qui est desor l’os,	and place another larger woolen thread over the flesh that is above the bone,
et estent le chief, si que tu traies la char corrumpue au desoz,	and are the head, so that you draw out the corruption below,
et descuevre la char sus le leu ou tu vues soier, que li soie ne blece la char;	and uncover the flesh above the place where you see it is rotting, so that the rot does not affect the healthy flesh;
et met .i. tison ou une tauble desoz l’os por mues coper la char corrumpue;	and put a burning brand or a hot table under the bone to cover the corrupted flesh;
et covient tant soier com on puet veoir et sentir la corruption, et soier ancor autre fois.	and one must cut as much as one can see and feel the corruption, and cut again.
Et se li os est corrumpus, et n’apert mie, et li corruptions est en mileu ou en une partie,	And if the bone is broken and does not open, and the break is in the middle or in a part of it,
si descuevre la char toute; puis met .i. tison desoz,	and reveals all the flesh; then put a burning brand underneath,
et puis soie des l’une partie a l’autre la corruption, et soit li soieure dou lonc de la corruption .i. poc, si com nos avons dit;	and then cut from one side of the break to the other, and make the cut as deep as the length of the break, as we have said;
et se li corruptions est en la jointure, si cope la jointure corrumpue, et soie l’os ou elle contient de l’autre part;	and if the break is in the joint, then cut through the joint and cut out the bone on the other side;
et se li corruptions est en la continuation des .ij. jointes, si n’i a autre angien que dou coper;	and if the dislocation is in the continuation of the two joints, there is no other remedy but to cut;
et se li corruptions est ou poignil de la main, ou ou poignil dou piet, si est mout fort celle chose,	and if the dislocation is at the base of the hand or the foot, it is very serious,
mais toutevoie il covient que tu enquieres celle corrosion, coment elle t’apert;	but nevertheless you should inquire into the dislocation, how it appears to you;
et la mundifie en toutes les manieres que tu pues, mais que li voine ou li nerf ne te faicent contraire;	and cleanse it in every way you can, but do not let the vein or nerve cause you discomfort;
et saiches que li incisoire et les soies por coper ces os sont maintes, selonc l’assise des os et l’aparance d’ous,	and know that there are many types of knives and scissors for cutting bone, depending on the structure of the bones and the appearance of the teeth.
et lor grossece et lor subtiliteit, et lor grandor et lor petitece, et lor duresce;	their thickness and thinness, their length and shortness, and their hardness;
et por ceu covient il apareillier a chescune semblance d’ovraige son estrument;	and for this reason, one must prepare an instrument for each type of work;
et saiches que l’uevre te moustrera l’estrument dont tu avras mestier, selonc la conissance de cest art,	and know that the work will show you the instrument you need, according to your knowledge of this art,
et le tesmoignaige des manieres des maladies;	and the testimony of the ways of diseases;
si porpense l’estrument dont tu as mestier selonc ceu qu’il le covient.	then prepare the instrument you need according to what is appropriate.
dou feu	by fire
Li chiés porrissent ou par cause dedens, ou par cause defuer;	The shoulders may dislocate due to internal causes or external causes;
et quant tu avras medicinee celle corrosion par la cure des medicines, et il ne profitent mie,	and when you have treated this corrosion with the cure of medicines, and they do not help,
si covient coper celui membre jusques au leu ou li corrosion vient,	then you should cover the limb up to the place where the corrosion occurs,
si que li malaides eschaipe par ceu de la mort, ou par la malice, qui est plus grans, de la defaute dou membre;	so that the patient escapes either by death or, which is worse, by disability due to the fault of the limb;
et li signes si est que li membres devient noir, si qu’il semble qu’il soit ars dou feu,	and the signs are that the limb becomes black and appears burnt by fire,
et porrist aprés la noiror, puis va celle corrosions de membre em membre,	and then comes darkness, followed by the腐食 of limb to limb,
et prent par tout le cors; si te haste dou coper,	and spreads throughout the body; so hasten to cover,
et se c’est par la percussion d’aucunes venimouses bestes, si com scorpion de mer et wivre et semblans,	and if it is from the sting of venomous beasts, such as scorpions, vipers, and similar creatures,
se li corrosion est au chief dou doi, si le cope, et ne li doner mie espaice de venir jusc’a la main.	if the腐食 is on the head, then cover it, and do not give it any space to reach the hand.
Et s’elle vient jusc’a la main, si la cope a la jointe, si que la corrosion ne viegne jusc’a bras;	And if it comes to the hand, then the cupping glass at the joint so that the scorching does not reach the arm;
et s’elle vient au bras, si le cope au coute; et s’elle passe le coute, c’est li mors,	and if it comes to the arm, then cup at the elbow; and if it passes the elbow, that is death,
et n’i vaut amenistremens fuers que li quantitez de sa vertut;	and there is no remedy for this except in accordance with the quantity of its virtue;
et tot ensi fai quant li corrosion vient ou piet: s’elle vient en la premiere jointe, si la cope aprés l’autre jointe;	And thus it is done when scorching comes to the foot: if it comes to the first joint, then cup after the other joint;
et s’elle vient ou piet, si cope tout le piet;	and if it comes to the foot, cut off the whole foot;
et s’elle monte en la jambe, si cope a la jointure dou genoil;	and if it rises to the leg, cut at the knee joint;
et s’elle vient desus le genoil, si n’i a autre engien que dou lassier le malaide a mort;	and if it comes above the knee, there is no other remedy but to kill the patient with a blow;
et li maniere dou coper ou dou soier le membre si est que tu le lie desus et desoz,	and the way to cut off the limb whether above or below, is that you tie it above and below,
et estende uns menistres l’un des liiens aval, et uns autres ministres l’autre liien amont,	and one minister extends one of the lines downstream, and another minister extends the other line upstream,
et tu dessevre la char qui est entre les .ij. liiens a .i. spatumile large, tant que li os soit descovers;	and you loosen the skin that is between the two lines to the width of a finger, as far as the bone is uncovered;
puis le cope ou soie, et met de chescune part .i. drapeil de lin, si que li soie ne touche le leu sain,	then the thread or silk, and place a piece of linen on each side, so that the thread does not touch the healthy area,
et viegne au malaide autre lesion et aposteme chaus.	and bring about another injury and abscess.
Et se decorremens de sanc vient quant tu oevres, si cauterize le leu hastanment,	And if bleeding occurs when you operate, cauterize the site aggressively,
ou tu met sus aucunes poudres restraignans; puis revien a ta medicine tant qu’elle soit acomplie,	or apply some restraining powders; then return to your treatment until it is complete,
puis lie le membre navreit d’un liien covenauble, et le cure tant qu’il soit sanez;	then bind the injured member with a suitable bandage, and treat it until it is healed;
et je te conterai k’il avint a .i. home en som piet:	and I will tell you what happened to a man in a dream:
il li avint une noiror qui sembloit arsure de feu,	there happened to him a darkness which looked like a burn from fire,
et celle corrosion vint premier en son doi dou piet, tant qu’elle porprist tout le piet;	and this corrosion came first in his right foot, until it affected the whole foot;
et quant li hons vit la corrosion, si se hasta de coper le piet, et fut sanez;	and when the man saw the corrosion, he covered the foot and it healed;
et lonc tens aprés li revint li corrosion ou doi de la main, et il vint a moi,	and long after that, the corrosion returned in his hand, and he came to me,
et je li mis sus choses repercussives aprés la mundification dou cors, et ne pot cesser li corrosions;	and I put on things that cause reverberation after cleansing the body, but he could not stop the corrosion;
et il vot que je li copasse la main, et je ne vou, que je avoie esperance de repercuter la matiere;	and he asked me to cut off his hand, but I did not want to because I had hope of reverberating the matter;
et doutai ausi que se je tailloie sa main, qu’il ne morist,	and I doubted that if I cut off his hand, he would die,
car li vertus de l’ome estoit foible; et il se despera toz, et revint en sa terre,	because the strength of the man was weak; and he despaired altogether, and returned to his land,
et se hasta de coper sa main, et fut sanez;	and he wrapped his hand, and was healed;
et je n’ai ceu conteit fuers que por ceu c’on faice autreteil, s’on en a mestier.	I have not included the translation of this line as it is not part of the text you provided for translation.
Aucune fois vient aposteme en leu charnut, et demore si longement qu’il fait grant assemblee de bowe;	At times, an abscess forms in a fleshy area and persists so long that it causes a great gathering of pus.
et puis ront et perce, et en saut li bowe, et demoure li leus vuis, ausi com uns vasselz;	Then they open and discharge, and the area remains hollow, just as with vessels.
et li cuir qui est desus est ausi subtilz com .i. drapelz deliiez,	and the skin on top is as thin as a loose napkin,
et ne corront mie jusc’a l’os, ne jusc’au nerf, et telz maladie si est apelee «sain»,	and it does not reach the bone or the nerve, and such a disease is called 'healthy',
et n’est mie apelee «fistule»;	and is not called 'fistula';
mais s’elle est si alongie qu’elle viegne jusc’a l’os em parfont, si est apelee «fistule»;	but if it is so long that it reaches the bone, then it is called 'fistula'.;
et li cuire si est que tu cope celui cuir tout entor, et meismement quant il est subtilz, ausi com uns drapelz;	and cook it so you wrap the hide all around, especially when it is thin, just like a cloth;
et ne s’aert mie por sa corruption.	and do not worry about its spoilage.
Et se tu as fiance que li cuirs s’aerde, et li corruption n’est mie en parfont,	And if you are worried that the hide will rot, and the spoilage is not complete,
et li cuir est espés de char, si le cure de clistere ensi:	and the hide is thick with flesh, then treat it thus:
regarde se li seins est grans, et li bowe qui en ist est de puant odor,	examine whether the breasts are swollen, and if there is a foul-smelling discharge from them.
adonques le clisterize de medicine egiptiaine qui est ensi faite:	then administer the Egyptian medicated enema made as follows:
prenez aisil, et oile, et litargire, igalment, et metez cuire en .i. vassel au feu,	take alum, oil, and litharge, in equal parts, and mix them together, heating the mixture in a vessel over fire,

et en clisterize lou sein, et estraint le pertus;	and use it as an enema on the breast, and constrict the orifice;
et laisse la medicine ens par .ij. houres, puis l’estrai en espreignant;	and let the medication remain inside for about two hours, then remove it by squeezing it out;
fai ce mout de fois, tant que li seins soit mondefiiez, et soit ostee li puor;	do this as many times as necessary until the breast is deflated and the swelling has gone down;
et aucune fois est clisterizeis d’aigue de cendres,	and sometimes they are cauterized with water and ashes,
quant ceste medicine n’est presens, et est que tu preignes cendres de fust de vigne, et giete aigue desus,	when this medicine is not present, and you should grind vine wood to ashes, and pour water over it,

et se li malaides ne le puet soffrir, ne la medicine egiptiaine ne l’aigue de cendres,	and if the patient cannot endure it, nor the Egyptian medicine, nor the water and ashes,
si le clisterize d’aigue et de miel ou il ait un poc de litargire broiet;	if he enemas with water and honey or if he has a little litarge powder;
ou tu la clistirize de miel et de vin melleit, que li mielz ait proprieteit de mundifiier et de laver,	or you can enema him with honey and sweet wine, so that the honey has the property of cleaning and washing,
et li vins fait aerdre le sain;	and the wine causes sweating;
et quant tu as ce fait, et tu as fiance que li seins est bien mundifiiez,	and when you have done this, and you trust that the intestines are well cleaned,
si le clisterize de ceu que fait naistre char en li,	if the enema is of that which causes flatulence within him,

Car quant li bowe est en parfont, si n’i laisse enjanrer char;	For when the bowels are full, one must not eat food.
et se tu ne pues coper lou sein desoz si com tu vues,	and if you cannot cover the breast underneath as you wish,

car quant li bowe est parfont, si n’i laisse enjanrer char	for when the bowels are full, one must not eat food.

et pren warde se li patiens sent dolor ou nom, et s’il i a aposteme ou non,	take note if the patient feels pain or not, and if there is an abscess or not,
et quant ta medicine s’est en teil maniere estendue et tu vois la nature que saut sus le pertus dou sein,	and when the medicine has spread in this way and you see that the nature of the wound on the breast
si saiches que li seins s’aert ja, et aproche li santez;	if you know that the breast is open and approaching healing;
et puis le deslie le matin, ou le tier jor, et quant tu delies la plaie,	and then loosen it in the morning, or the third day, and when you loosen the wound,
si chainge .i. autre drapeil, et renovele l’oignement.	change a different cloth, and renew the ointment.
Et se li seins giete bowe indigeste aprés maint jor, saiches que li seins ne s’aert mie.	And if the breast milk flows strongly after many days, you can be sure that the breast will not dry up.
Et se venins subtilz cort aprés lonc tens, si ne te desperer mie de la santeit,	And if subtle poisons spread after a long time, do not despair of your health,
car li santez aproche. Car il i a homes cui tarde enjanremens de char en ses plaies, et de ces que font le contraire;	for the saints are drawing near. For there are men whose wounds heal slowly, and others who heal quickly.
et se bowe indigeste saut dou sein aprés maint jor, saiches que li seins ne s’aert mie;	and if a lump in the breast does not disappear after many days, know that it will not go away on its own;
et se li seins tarde d’aerdre, et est porloigniez, si ajoste medicines sechans moistes en substance et seches en vertut,	and if the breasts are slow to dry up, and are distant, then apply medicines which are moist in substance but dry in virtue,
si com oignement diafinit, car il i a grant partie de vitriole, et c’est li derriene medicine;	such as an ointment containing vitriol, for it is the best medicine.
pren oignement dyafinit, et le font avec oile roset, et l’arose de viel vin igal en substance;	take a definite ointment, and make it with rose oil, and rose wine of equal substance.
puis le confit et en use; et ceu meisme fait mielz cuit engroissiez,	then cook it and use it; and in the same way, make cooked honey thickener
quant oignemens dyafinit n’est presens,	when a definite ointment is not present,
ou tu pren mirre et aloen et encens, et le broie, et le poudre sus le miel quant il est sor le feu;	or take myrrh and aloe and incense, and grind them up into powder over the honey while it is on the fire;
et puis en glue .i. drapel, et l’estent sor le sein, et aucune fois i aministre on aristologe longe,	and then apply a poultice and place it over the chest, and sometimes administer a long arystologus,
et racines de lis celeste, qui est ausi com farine de veces et centoire;	and roots of the celestial lily, which is like flour of vetch and centaury;
et en use de simples ou de compostes: broie les, et en fai poudre, et met sus le miel que j’ai dit, et en use;	and use simple or composite herbs: grind them into powder, and place them on the honey I have mentioned, and use it;
et se li cure est alongie, et n’est curez par ceste cure,	and if the wound is long, and not healed by this treatment,
adonc saiches que la corruptions est em parfont, et fait empression en l’os, ou as membres durs, ou as liemens;	then you know that the corruption is complete, and makes an impression on the bone, or in the limbs, or in the tissues;
si le cure de la cure de fistule, si com nos avons dit ci devant.	if the treatment of the fistula, as we have said before.
de l’aposteme de l’ungle	of the nail abscess
Panarice est un aposteme que naist desoz l’ungle dou pouchiet de la main,	Panarice is an abscess that arises under the nail of the thumb of the hand,
ou dou piet, ou par aventure naist en autres dois;	or from the foot, or perhaps it grows in other parts of the body;
et quant il est envielliez, et on n’i prent garde, si i vient .i. aposteme chaus,	and when it is infected and left untreated, an abscess forms;
et corront et giete bowe tant qu’elle corront la racine de l’ungle, et par aventure la corront toute;	and they grow and rot until they reach the root of the nail, and sometimes they rot the entire nail;
et vient li corrosions jusc’a l’os, tant qu’il i vient dolor puant, et est li chiés dou doi larges, et est li color fuxe.	and the corrosion reaches the bone, causing a foul-smelling pain, and the toe becomes swollen, and the colour is yellow.
Quant tu le cures si com nos avons dit en la division, et li cure ne profite mie,	When you treat it as we have said in the division, and the treatment does not help
si covient que tu copes a i. fer toute la superfluiteit qui est demoree de l’ungle,	you must cut off all the excess which is hanging from the nail,
puis cauterize la plaie aprés.	then cauterize the wound afterward.
Li cauteres est mout grans aide se li os est sains, et li ungle est sainne;	Cautery is a great help if the bone and nail are healthy;
et se li ungle apresse la char ens, et l’encomence a poindre, et la blece,	and if the nail presses against the flesh, and begins to point, and the blister,
si covient que tu mettes lou rait desoz l’ungle que point la char,	then you should put the thread under the nail that is pointing at the flesh,
et la boute en haut, et cope celi char subtilment et legierement,	and pull it upwards gently and slowly,
et met sus le remenant de la char medicines ardans et corrosives por oster tout;	and put on the remaining flesh burning and corrosive medications to remove everything;
puis le cure d’oignemens tant qu’il soit sanez.	then treat the boil with poultices until it is healed.
Et se li corrosion est en l’os, si le cope, et trai fuer, car tant com li os corrumpus i est, si ne puet saner;	And if the corrosion is in the bone, cut it out and draw it out, for as long as the bone is corrupted, it cannot heal.
et se tu vois le doi corrumpre, si le cope en .i. des nous si com il est devant dit,	And if you see the tooth corrupt, pull it out as previously described,
puis le cure tant qu’il soit sanez;	then treat the boil until it is healed;
et s’il est ferus, et boutez, et il sent grant dolor, si covient que tu le sainnes premier;	and if it is wild, and biting, and it feels great pain, then you must heal it first;
puis cope l’ungle dou spatumile agut en taillant de travers desus,	then cut the nail of the big toe diagonally from above,
et warde que li taille ne viegne jusc’a la char qui est desoz l’ungle, car li malaides sentiroit trop grant dolor;	and be careful that the cut does not reach the flesh under the nail, for the patient would feel too much pain;
et s’il avient, si met chose sus qui apaise.	and if it happens, apply something to soothe it.
la dolor dou sourdoit de la main	the pain of a deaf person's hand
Li dois ajostez qui naist en mains d’aucuns homes par aventure est toz charnus,	You must adjust that which is born in the hands of some men by chance, and is entirely fleshy,
et par aventure i a teil ou il a osses, et aucune fois i a ungle,	and sometimes it has bones, and sometimes only nails,
et aucun d’aus naissent en la racine de la jointure, ou li naissance est en aucuns nous des dois.	and some are born at the base of the joint, where the growth is in one of the fingers.
Cil qui naist en aucune nout dou doi ne se muet,	Those who are born with a hernia in their groin should not move,
et cil qui naist a la jointure dou doi, par aventure se muet;	and those who are born with a hernia at the junction of the groin, by chance may move;
la taille de celui qui est charnus si est legiere, en teil maniere:	the size of one who is fleshy is light, in such a way:
taille le en sa racine d’un large spatumile.	cut it at its root with a wide spatula.
Cil qui naist en la racine de la jointure si est grief a curer: si te tien dou coper.	He who is born at the root of the joint, if you hold it tight.
En celui qui naist ou doit au derrien nout, si covient que tu copes premier la char reondement jusc’a l’os,	In him who is born where the anus should be, you must first press the flesh around the bone.
puis cope l’os a une soie convenable a ceu, puis le cure tant qu’il soit sanez.	Then press the bone with a suitable instrument, then treat it until it is healed.
